id='poem_sentence_13_9369'>自谓经过旧不迷，安知峰<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作岑）</span>壑今来变。<div id='poem_sentence_13_9369_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_9082_0'>① （题下一有怨字，一作息妫怨，时年二十）。（《本事诗》云：“宁王宅左，有卖饼者妻，纤白明媚。王一见属意，厚遗其夫，取之。宠惜逾等，岁馀，因问曰：‘汝复忆饼师否？’使见之，其妻注视，双泪垂颊，若不胜情。王座客十馀人，皆当时文士，无不悽异。王命赋诗，维诗先成，座客无敢继者。王乃归饼师，以终其志。”）</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_9082'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9082'>莫以今时<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作朝）</span>宠，能忘<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>旧<span id='poem_sentence_20_1366577_comment'></div>苟以文墨抵罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366577_comment'></div>除名为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366577_comment'></div>削迹于野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366577_comment'></div>杜陵解印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366577_comment'></div>时卖故侯之瓜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366577_comment'></div>彭泽无官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366577_comment'></div>讵有公田之黍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366577_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1366577", 1366577, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>牵衣肘见</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366577_comment'></div>步雪履穿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366577_comment'></div>获戾由中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366577_comment'></div>是贫非病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366577_comment'></div>海内乂安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366577_comment'></div>尽登仁寿之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366577_comment'></div>犹下哀怜之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366577_comment'></div>万方有罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366577_comment'></div>与之更新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366577_comment'></div>百寮失职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366577_comment'></div>使复其位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366577_comment'></div>降邑宰为舆尉。<div id='poem_sentence_50_1366577_comment'></div>且有同时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366577_comment'></div>时工部侍郎萧公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366577_comment'></div>词翰之宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366577_comment'></div>籯金盛业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366577_comment'></div>克传丞相文儒。<div class='inline' class='inlineComment2'>（一作开变）</span>化生<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(920, "poem_sentence_3_9292")'>巨灵</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_9292_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_9292'>右足踏方止<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作山）</span>，左手推削成。<div id='poem_sentence_4_9292_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_9292'>天地忽开拆，大河注东溟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_9292_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_9292'>遂为西峙岳<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作岳崎）</span>，雄雄镇秦京。<div id='poem_sentence_6_9292_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_9292'>大君包覆载，至德被群生。<div id='poem_sentence_7_9292_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_9292'>上帝伫昭告，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_9292", 9292, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>金天</span>思奉迎。<div id='poem_sentence_8_9292_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_9292'>人<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作神）</span>祇望幸久，何独禅云亭。<div id='poem_sentence_9_9292_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_9292'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_9292_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=730&endYear=730')">730年</a>　开元十七年十一月，任某子官羽林将军，护卫玄宗谒五陵，受赠父丹州刺史，母加赠河东郡君，因改葬立碑，作神道碑。作品：故右豹韬卫长史赐丹州刺史任君神道碑。<div id='poem_1366589' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366589' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366589?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故右豹韬卫长史赐丹州刺史任君神道碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（730年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366589")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366589_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366589'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366589'>君讳某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366589_comment'></div>字某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366589_comment'></div>其先奚仲之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366589_comment'></div>于商为上卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366589_comment'></div>世有功烈于诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366589_comment'></div>氏则任郁为著族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366589_comment'></div>后有官于京兆者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366589_comment'></div>子孙因家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366589_comment'></div>今为万年县人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366589_comment'></div>远祖某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366589_comment'></div>汉河东太守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366589_comment'></div>曾祖某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366589_comment'></div>周清河太守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366589_comment'></div>光复旧职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366589_comment'></div>异世而同符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366589_comment'></div>祖某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366589_comment'></div>隋梁州南郑县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366589_comment'></div>父某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366589_comment'></div>皇石州离石县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366589_comment'></div>不坠象贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366589_comment'></div>一门而二凫舄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366589_comment'></div>皆为政以德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366589_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1366589", 1366589, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>遗爱</span>在人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366589_comment'></div>能高其门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366589_comment'></div>必有兴者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366589_comment'></div>虽不当代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366589_comment'></div>果生达人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366589_comment'></div>君离石府君之第某子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366589_comment'></div>膺一贤之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366589_comment'></div>钟累叶之善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366589_comment'></div>忠孝自得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366589_comment'></div>禀乎天姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366589_comment'></div>诗礼辅成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366589_comment'></div>润以庭训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366589_comment'></div>文含四始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366589_comment'></div>雕虫之技附庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366589_comment'></div>武有七德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366589_comment'></div>啼猿之术居外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366589_comment'></div>明经者皓首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366589_comment'></div>弱岁成儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366589_comment'></div>达法者腐唇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366589_comment'></div>端居晓吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366589_comment'></div>以乡贡明经擢第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366589_comment'></div>解褐益州新都尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366589_comment'></div>居无何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366589_comment'></div>丁母忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366589_comment'></div>庐以长号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366589_comment'></div>泪少于血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366589_comment'></div>杖而后起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366589_comment'></div>骨馀于形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366589_comment'></div>弹琴不成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366589_comment'></div>从先王之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366589_comment'></div>捧筐便恸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366589_comment'></div>有终身之哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366589_comment'></div>服阕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366589_comment'></div>授左金吾卫兵曹参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366589_comment'></div>转左卫录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366589_comment'></div>又迁右豹韬卫长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366589_comment'></div>王乐为用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366589_comment'></div>率武夫以捍城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366589_comment'></div>人爱其才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366589_comment'></div>称君子之为卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366589_comment'></div>方将冠章甫之冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366589_comment'></div>衣逢掖之衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366589_comment'></div>奏议云台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366589_comment'></div>论政赤墀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366589_comment'></div>一见天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366589_comment'></div>必为之前席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366589_comment'></div>三说大臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366589_comment'></div>必为之解印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366589_comment'></div>若端委以相六合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366589_comment'></div>尽宅心于帝庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366589_comment'></div>授钺以董<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_72_1366589", 1366589, "Clauses/72/Comments/0")'>八蛮</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366589_comment'></div>可传首于魏阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366589_comment'></div>然后挂冠东郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366589_comment'></div>拂衣五湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366589_comment'></div>高蹈烟虹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366589_comment'></div>笑谢圭组。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366589_comment'></div>天命不祐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366589_comment'></div>沮我良策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366589_comment'></div>春秋若干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366589_comment'></div>以某年月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366589_comment'></div>寝疾卒于永兴里第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366589_comment'></div>某年月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366589_comment'></div>葬于京兆神禾原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366589_comment'></div>礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366589_comment'></div>嗣子曰某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366589_comment'></div>善继先志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1366589_comment'></div>克成厥家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1366589_comment'></div>多艺多才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1366589_comment'></div>安英实选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1366589_comment'></div>匪□实宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1366589_comment'></div>十城之价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1366589_comment'></div>不以力闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1366589_comment'></div>万夫之敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1366589_comment'></div>命同御座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1366589_comment'></div>汉帝以恩待故人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1366589_comment'></div>超将中军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1366589_comment'></div>先轸以才登元帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1366589_comment'></div>以某年月日从驾谒五陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1366589_comment'></div>天子若曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1366589_comment'></div>自古明王因心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1366589_comment'></div>以孝待人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1366589_comment'></div>由已以施物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1366589_comment'></div>故休戚共。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1366589_comment'></div>忧乐同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1366589_comment'></div>其赠羽林将军任某父使持节丹州诸军事丹州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1366589_comment'></div>敬其事则命以始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1366589_comment'></div>宠其身以及其亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1366589_comment'></div>明主所以尽心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1366589_comment'></div>忠臣所以尽力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1366589_comment'></div>故羊舌职悦是赏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1366589_comment'></div>陈力异代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1366589_comment'></div>官成圣朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1366589_comment'></div>修文下泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1366589_comment'></div>名在天爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1366589_comment'></div>前贤阴德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1366589_comment'></div>虽贻庆于后昆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1366589_comment'></div>嗣子扬名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1366589_comment'></div>乃大显于先父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1366589_comment'></div>养则致乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1366589_comment'></div>没而有称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1366589_comment'></div>昔也为士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1366589_comment'></div>享唯将军之食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1366589_comment'></div>今则典邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1366589_comment'></div>葬亦诸侯之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1366589_comment'></div>皇帝命之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1366589_comment'></div>太史书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1366589_comment'></div>报昊天之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1366589_comment'></div>曾举世未有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1366589_comment'></div>岂与夫手树行槚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1366589_comment'></div>躬庐长松。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1366589_comment'></div>负土成坟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1366589_comment'></div>佣身以葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1366589_comment'></div>匹夫之孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1366589_comment'></div>同年而语哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1366589_comment'></div>君少有大略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1366589_comment'></div>长而能贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1366589_comment'></div>安于仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1366589_comment'></div>乐于善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1366589_comment'></div>厚生以俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1366589_comment'></div>守智以愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1366589_comment'></div>视事所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1366589_comment'></div>笔研盈庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1366589_comment'></div>其力文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1366589_comment'></div>容膝之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1366589_comment'></div>图书满屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1366589_comment'></div>其嗜学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1366589_comment'></div>八体之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1366589_comment'></div>右军曾未知翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1366589_comment'></div>五弦之妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1366589_comment'></div>中散何擅于琴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1366589_comment'></div>以礼庇身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1366589_comment'></div>以清守官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1366589_comment'></div>惟邦之彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1366589_comment'></div>惟国之翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1366589_comment'></div>夫人河东裴氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1366589_comment'></div>始以某为光禄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1366589_comment'></div>封河东郡君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1366589_comment'></div>及是又赠河东郡太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1366589_comment'></div>子之忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1366589_comment'></div>由母之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1366589_comment'></div>母以子贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1366589_comment'></div>不亦宜乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1366589_comment'></div>司文者执简以往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1366589_comment'></div>刊石旌德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1366589_comment'></div>其词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1366589_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_167_1366589'>嶭侯之裔兮代济其美不陨其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1366589_comment'></div>是生硕德兮为世作程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1366589_comment'></div>忠不祐孝不福兮早谢休名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1366589_comment'></div>身为士兮子为卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1366589_comment'></div>大将羽林兮统天兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1366589_comment'></div>天子宠兮为崇荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1366589_comment'></div>赠我<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_173_1366589", 1366589, "Clauses/173/Comments/0")'>武符</span>兮赐我专城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1366589_comment'></div>青松寂寂兮昼无人声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1366589_comment'></div>狗不吠兮鸡不鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1366589_comment'></div>苍茫千古兮孰云旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1366589_comment'></div>赖孝子兮扬音英。</div><div id='poem_sentence_177_1366589_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=731&endYear=731')">731年</a>　妻亡约在是年。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=732&endYear=732')">732年</a>　从弟王蕃游淮南，有诗送之。作品：送从弟蕃游淮南。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《文苑英华》题作“送从弟叔游淮南座上成”）</span><div id='poem_9266' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9266' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9266?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_2_9266'>高义难自隐，明时宁<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(6011, "poem_sentence_2_9266")'>陆沈</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_9266_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_9266'>岛夷九州外，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_9266", 9266, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>泉馆</span>三山深。<div id='poem_sentence_3_9266_comment'></div></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=733&endYear=733')">733年</a>　与严挺之、徐峤交往，有诗。作品：酬严少尹徐舍人见过不遇。<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈铁民《王维集校注》认为：严少尹即严武，严挺之之子；徐舍人即徐浩。）</span>晚春严少尹与诸公见过。赠徐中书望终南山。<div id='poem_9143' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9143' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9143?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和尹谏议史馆山池<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（737年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_9143")'>王维</a></span><br ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=737&endYear=737')">737年</a>　与萧嵩、张九龄、韩休、杜暹、王邱、裴耀卿等于韦氏逍遥谷宴集，作序文。作品：暮春太师丞相诸公于韦氏逍遥谷宴集序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（逍遥谷，韦嗣立别业，在骊山清虚原幽栖谷。）</span><div id='poem_1366571' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366571' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366571?labeling=true' target='_blank'>暮春太师左右丞相诸公于韦氏逍遥谷宴集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（737年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366571")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366571_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366571'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366571'>山有姑射。人盖方外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366571_comment'></div>海有蓬瀛。地非宇下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366571_comment'></div>逍遥谷天都近者。王官有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366571_comment'></div>不废大伦。存乎小隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366571_comment'></div>迹崆峒而身拖朱绂。朝承明而暮宿青霭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366571_comment'></div>故可尚也。先天之君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366571_comment'></div>俾人在宥。欢心格于上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366571_comment'></div>喜气降为阳春。时则有若太子太师徐国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366571_comment'></div>左丞相稷山公。右丞相始兴公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366571_comment'></div>少师宜阳公。少保崔公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366571_comment'></div>特进邓公。吏部尚书武都公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366571_comment'></div>礼部尚书杜公。宾客王公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366571_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1366571", 1366571, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>黼衣方领</span>。垂珰珥笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366571_comment'></div>诏有不名。命无下拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366571_comment'></div>熙天工者。坐而论道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366571_comment'></div>典邦教者。官司其方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366571_comment'></div>相与察天地之和。人神之泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366571_comment'></div>听于朝则雅颂矣。问于野则赓歌矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366571_comment'></div>乃曰。猗哉至理之代也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366571_comment'></div>吾徒可以酒合宴乐。考击钟鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366571_comment'></div>退于彤庭。撰辰择地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366571_comment'></div>右班剑。骖六驺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366571_comment'></div>画轮载毂。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1366571", 1366571, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>羽幢</span>先路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366571_comment'></div>以诣夫逍遥谷焉。神皋藉其绿草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366571_comment'></div>骊山启于朱户。渭之美竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366571_comment'></div>鲁之嘉树。云出于栋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366571_comment'></div>水环其室。灞陵下连乎菜地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366571_comment'></div>新丰半入于冢林。馆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1366571", 1366571, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>层巅</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366571_comment'></div>槛侧径。师古节俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366571_comment'></div>惟新丹垩。岩谷先曙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366571_comment'></div>羲和不能信其时。芳卉<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作卉木）</span>后春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366571_comment'></div>勾芒不能一其令。桃<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作花）</span>径窈窕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366571_comment'></div>蘅皋涟漪<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作超忽）</span>。骖御延伫于丛薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366571_comment'></div>佩玉升降于苍翠。于是<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1366571", 1366571, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>外仆</span>告次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366571_comment'></div>兽人献鲜。樽以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1366571", 1366571, "Clauses/69/Comments/0")'>大罍</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366571_comment'></div>烹用五鼎。木器拥肿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366571_comment'></div>即天姿以为饰。沼毛蘋蘩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366571_comment'></div>在山羞而可荐。伶人在位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366571_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1366571", 1366571, "Clauses/76/Comments/0")'>曼姬</span>始縠。齐瑟慷慨于座右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366571_comment'></div>赵舞裴回于白云。衮旒松风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366571_comment'></div>珠翠烟露。日在濛汜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366571_comment'></div>群山夕岚。犹且濯缨清歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366571_comment'></div>据梧高咏。与松乔为伍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366571_comment'></div>是羲皇上人。且三代之后而其君帝舜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366571_comment'></div>九服之内而其俗华胥。上客则冠冕巢由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366571_comment'></div>主人则弟兄元恺。是四美同乎一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366571_comment'></div>废而不书。罪在司礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366571_comment'></div>窃思<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作贤）</span>楚傅。常诣茅堂之居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366571_comment'></div>仰谢右军。忽序兰亭之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366571_comment'></div>盖不获命。岂曰能贤。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=738&endYear=738')">738年</a>　夏末秋初，为崔希逸上奏玄宗，请让其女落发奉佛，以忏悔他与乞力徐盟誓失约。作品：赞佛文。<div id='poem_1366581' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366581' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366581'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366581'>窃以真如妙宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366581_comment'></div>具十方而无成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366581_comment'></div>涅般至功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366581_comment'></div>满四生而不度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366581_comment'></div>故无边大照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366581_comment'></div>不照得空有之深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366581_comment'></div>万法偕行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366581_comment'></div>无行为满足之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366581_comment'></div>惟兹化佛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366581_comment'></div>即具三身。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1366581_comment'></div>实藉津梁法相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366581_comment'></div>脱落尘容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366581_comment'></div>始于度门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366581_comment'></div>左散骑常侍摄御史中丞崔公第十五娘子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366581_comment'></div>于多劫来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366581_comment'></div>植众德本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366581_comment'></div>以般若力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366581_comment'></div>生菩提家。<div id='poem_sentence_70_1366581_comment'></div>长为佛母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366581_comment'></div>郎君娘子等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366581_comment'></div>住诫性为孝顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366581_comment'></div>用□德为道场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366581_comment'></div>将遍众生之慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366581_comment'></div>回同一子之想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366581_comment'></div>又愿普同法界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366581_comment'></div>尽及有情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366581_comment'></div>共此胜因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366581_comment'></div>俱登圣果。</div><div id='poem_sentence_80_1366581_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=738&endYear=738')">738年</a>　为崔希逸夫人李氏的亡父追荐冥福。作品：西方变画赞并序。<div id='poem_1366582' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366582' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366582?labeling=true' target='_blank'>西方净土变画赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（738年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366582")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366582_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1366582'>法身无对。非东西也。净土无所。离空有也。若依佛慧。既洗涤于六尘。未舍法求。厌如幻于三有。故大雄以不思议力。开方便门。我心犹疑。未认宝藏。商人既倦。且息化城。究境达于无生。因地从于有相。西方净土变者。左常侍摄御史中丞崔公夫人李氏奉为亡考故某官中祥之所作也。夫人门为士族之先。道为梵行之首。大师继踵。望尘而理印。命妇盈朝。闻风而素履。心王自在。万有皆如。顶法真空。一乘不立。以示见故。菩萨为胜鬘夫人。同解脱因。天女赞维摩长者。陟岵何至。哀哀缞绖。顺有漏法。泣血以居。念罔极恩。灭性非报。惟兹十力所护。岂与百身之赎。不宝缨络。资于绘素。图极乐国。象无上乐。法王安详。圣众围绕。湛然不动。疑过于往来。寂尔无闻。若离于言说。林分宝树。七重绕于香城。衣奉天花。六时散于金地。迦陵欲语。曼陁未落。众善普会。诸相具美。于是竭诚稽首。陨涕焚香。愿立功德。以备梯航。得彼佛身。常以慈悲为女。存乎法性。还在菩提之家。偈曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1366582_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366582'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366582'>稽首十方大<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1366582", 1366582, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>导师</span>。能于一法见多法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366582_comment'></div>以种种相导群生。其心本来无所动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366582_comment'></div>稽首无边法性海。功德无量不思议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366582_comment'></div>于已不色等无碍。不住有无亦不舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366582_comment'></div>我今深达真实空。知此色相体清净。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366582_comment'></div>愿以西方为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1366582", 1366582, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>导首</span>。往生极乐性自在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366582_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1366582_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=738&endYear=738')">738年</a>　与源同在崔希逸幕中，时崔已殁，源归岐州，有诗送之。作品：送岐州源长史归。<div id='poem_9179' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9179' class='poemTitle id='poem_title_9179_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_9179'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(6320, id='poem_sentence_0_9179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9179'>秋风正萧索，客散<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(6320, "poem_sentence_1_9179")'>孟尝</span>门。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=739&endYear=739')">739年</a>　道光禅师去世，为其塔作铭文并序。作品：大荐福寺大德道光禅师塔铭并序。<div id='poem_1366594' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366594' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_1366594_comment'></div>绵州巴西人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366594_comment'></div>其先有特有流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366594_comment'></div>若实有蜀。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=741&endYear=741')">741年</a>　隐居终南山，有诗赠张諲。作品：戏赠张五弟諲三首。<div id='poem_9243' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9243' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366598?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故任城县尉裴府君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（743年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366598")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366598_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366598'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366598'>天宝二年正月十二日。唐故鲁郡任城县尉河东裴府君卒于西京新昌坊私第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366598_comment'></div>享年三十九。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366598_comment'></div>君讳回。字玉温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366598_comment'></div>河东闻喜人也。曾祖宏泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366598_comment'></div>皇雍州录事参军。赠上党长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366598_comment'></div>祖思义。皇侍御史吏部员外左司郎中户部吏部侍郎河东郡太守晋城县开国子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366598_comment'></div>父扬珍。皇嶭王府骑曹参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366598_comment'></div>自晋已降。世为冠族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366598_comment'></div>令德不替。不至于君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366598_comment'></div>夫其事亲孝。兄弟顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366598_comment'></div>与朋友信。其从政公平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366598_comment'></div>而寿不中年。官才一命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366598_comment'></div>慈母在堂。诸弟未仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366598_comment'></div>儿未有识。女且婴孩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366598_comment'></div>妻夭于前。身殁于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366598_comment'></div>天可问邪。其若老亲何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366598_comment'></div>其若季仲诸孤何。生人之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366598_comment'></div>莫甚于是。家贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366598_comment'></div>祭以枣脯。殓以时服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366598_comment'></div>以某月日。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1366598", 1366598, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>祔葬</span>于凤栖原先府君之茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366598_comment'></div>呜呼。有河东裴子之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366598_comment'></div>志之盖古有之。继后之知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366598_comment'></div>亦何有哉。铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366598_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1366598'>一死万纪。终天不复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366598_comment'></div>为之奈何。哀哀恸哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366598_comment'></div>覆载至广。庶类繁育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366598_comment'></div>万物方春。而就于木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366598_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1366598_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=743&endYear=743')">743年</a>　秋，与王昌龄、王缙、裴迪等集会长安新昌坊昙壁上人院共同赋诗。作品：青龙寺昙壁上人兄院集。<div id='poem_9262' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9262' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9262?labeling=true' target='_blank'>青龙寺昙璧上人兄院集<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（743年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_9262")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_9262_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_9262_0'>① 并序。与王昌龄、裴迪、弟缙同作，序云江宁大兄，即昌龄也。</div></div></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_9262'>吾兄大开荫中，明彻物外，以定力胜敌、以惠用解严，深居僧坊，傍俯人里。高原陆地，下映芙蓉之池；竹林果园，中秀菩提之树。八极氛霁，万汇尘息，太虚寥廓，南山为之端倪。皇州苍茫，渭水贯于天地。经行之后，趺坐而閒。升堂梵筵，饵客香饭。不起而游览，不风而清凉。得世界于莲花，寄文章于贝叶。时江宁大兄持片石，命维序之，诗五韵，座上成。</div><div id='poem_preface_9262_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_9262'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9262'>高处敞招提，虚空讵有倪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9262'>坐看南陌骑，下听秦城鸡。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9262'>眇眇孤烟起，芊芊远树齐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_9262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_9262'>青山万井外，落日五陵西。<div id='poem_sentence_3_9262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_9262'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_9262", 9262, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>眼界</span>今无染，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_9262", 9262, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>心空</span>安可迷。<div id='poem_sentence_4_9262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_9262'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_9262_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=743&endYear=743')">743年</a>　韦陟贬为襄阳太守，有诗寄之。作品：奉寄韦太守陟。<div id='poem_9260' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9260' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9260?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉寄韦太守陟</a><span class='authorDate'>（743年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_9260")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_9260_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_9260'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9260'>荒城自萧索，万里山河空。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9260'>天高秋日迥，嘹唳闻归鸿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9260'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_9260", 9260, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>寒塘</span>映衰草，高馆落疏桐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_9260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_9260'>临此岁方晏，顾景咏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_9260", 9260, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>悲翁</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_9260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_9260'>故人不可见，寂寞平陵东。<div id='poem_sentence_4_9260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_9260'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_9260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_9260'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(9260)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=743&endYear=743')">743年</a>　丘为进士及第，往唐州任职，有诗送之。作品：送丘为往唐州。<div id='poem_9171' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_9171", 9171, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>四愁</span>连汉水，百口寄随人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9171'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_9171", 9171, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>槐色</span>阴清昼，杨花惹暮春。<div id='poem_sentence_2_9171_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_9171_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=743&endYear=743')">743年</a>　自上年秋居终南到天宝二年，作山水田园诗写终南山一带景物。作品：渭川田家。春中田园作。田家。早秋山中作。自大散以往深林密竹蹬道盘曲四五十里至黄牛岭见黄花川。新晴野望。青溪。冬晚对雪忆胡居士家。<div id='poem_9391' class='_poem'><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=744&endYear=744')">744年</a>　任库部员外郎。奉制作文。作品：奉和圣制圣札赐宰臣连珠词五首应制。<div id='poem_1366588' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366588' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366588?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和圣制圣劄赐宰臣连珠词五首应制</a><span class='authorDate'>（744年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366588")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366588_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366588'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366588'>臣闻大明驭宇。天地同符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366588_comment'></div>间气佐时。君臣协德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366588_comment'></div>故千年圣主。唐帝抚其宝图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366588_comment'></div>七德诸侯。周公为之元老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366588_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1366588'>臣闻有其才者效其职。重其任者竭其能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366588_comment'></div>故乐播大风。乃能调四气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366588_comment'></div>身骑列宿。于是运三光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366588_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1366588'>臣闻先天不违。德合于上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366588_comment'></div>事君尽力。功济于下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366588_comment'></div>故君臣同体于大道。庶人以康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366588_comment'></div>亿兆宅心于至仁。万邦乃固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366588_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1366588'>臣闻形之端者。影必随焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366588_comment'></div>声之善者。响必应焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366588_comment'></div>故偃武修文。皇天降之善气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366588_comment'></div>薄赋省役。后土报以丰年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366588_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1366588'>臣闻宣至理者文。悬之于日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366588_comment'></div>表圣言者字。动之以烟云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366588_comment'></div>故虞舜作歌。徒施于典策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366588_comment'></div>伏羲画卦。未类于昭回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366588_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1366588_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=744&endYear=744')">744年</a>　殷遥去世，有诗哭之。作品：哭殷遥二首。<div id='poem_9367' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9367' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=746&endYear=746')">746年</a>　为河西节度使王忠嗣作祭沙陁鄯国夫人文。作品：为王常侍祭沙陁鄯国夫人文。<div id='poem_1366609' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366609' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366609?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为王常侍祭沙陁鄯国夫人文</a><span class='authorDate'>（746年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366609")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366609_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366609'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366609'>维年月日朔。河西节度使左散骑常侍王公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366609_comment'></div>遣总管石抱玉。以酒牢之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366609_comment'></div>致祭于故沙陁鄯国夫人之灵。呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366609_comment'></div>惟此淑德。降于异域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366609_comment'></div>至性不师。天姿靡饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366609_comment'></div>礼容讵假于环佩。工艺非因于组织。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366609_comment'></div>行<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1366609", 1366609, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>闺训</span>于穹庐。成母仪于蕃国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366609_comment'></div>懿此<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1366609", 1366609, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>清范</span>。夫人之则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366609_comment'></div>沙陁令门。外家之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366609_comment'></div>呜呼。夫人归命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366609_comment'></div>干戈遂寝。子孙捍城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366609_comment'></div>国家高枕。居之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1366609", 1366609, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>右地</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366609_comment'></div>革其左衽。散辫垂鬟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366609_comment'></div>解裘衣锦。呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366609_comment'></div>降年不永。远日方临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366609_comment'></div>寂矣高堂。饮珠含王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366609_comment'></div>哀哉贵女。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1366609", 1366609, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>刃面</span>摧心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366609_comment'></div>呜呼。圣朝命我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366609_comment'></div>护此诸蕃。夫人所出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366609_comment'></div>天子加恩。能守汉制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366609_comment'></div>不效夷言。马无北首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366609_comment'></div>车必南辕。教义所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366609_comment'></div>忠信弥敦。实嘉内训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366609_comment'></div>用洁斯樽。尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366609_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1366609_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=747&endYear=747')">747年</a>　与苑咸交往。作品：苑舍人能书梵字兼达梵音皆曲尽其妙戏为之答。<div id='poem_9149' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9149' class='poemTitle class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_9149'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9674, "poem_allusion_9149")'>扬马</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_9149_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_9149'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9149'>名儒待诏满公车，才子为郎典石渠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9149'>莲花<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_9149", 9149, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>法藏</span>心<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_9149", 9149, "Clauses/2/Comments/1")'>悬悟</span>，贝叶经文手自书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9149'>楚<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>词共许胜<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_2_9149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_9149'>故旧相望在三事，愿君莫厌承明庐。<div id='poem_sentence_3_9149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_9149'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_9149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_9149'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_9149_0'>⑴ 《文苑》作岁，注云，集作楚，非</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_9149_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=747&endYear=747')">747年</a>　重酬苑咸。作品：重酬苑郎中。<div id='poem_9197' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9197' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9197?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重酬苑郎中<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序。时为库部员外）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（747年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_9197")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_9197_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_9197'>顷辄奉赠，忽枉见酬。叙末云：「且久不迁，因而嘲及。」诗落句云：「应同罗汉无名欲，故作冯唐老岁年。」亦解嘲之类也。</div><div id='poem_preface_9197_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_9197'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1358, "poem_allusion_9197")'>无私断埽门</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4781, "poem_allusion_9197")'>扬子解嘲</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5415, "poem_allusion_9197")'>冯唐</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_9197_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_9197'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9197'>何幸<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_9197", 9197, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>含香</span>奉至尊，多惭未报主人恩。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9197_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9197'>草木尽<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作岂）</span>能酬雨露，荣枯安敢问乾坤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9197_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9197'>仙郎有意怜同舍，丞相<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1358, "poem_sentence_2_9197")'>无私断埽门</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_9197_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_9197'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4781, "poem_sentence_3_9197")'>扬子解嘲</span>徒自遣，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5415, "poem_sentence_3_9197")'>冯唐</span>已老复何论<span class='inlineComment2'>（咸为李林甫记室，丞相，盖指李也）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_9197_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_9197'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_9197_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=747&endYear=747')">747年</a>　为作苗晋卿德政碑文。作品：魏郡太守河北采访处置使苗公德政碑。<div id='poem_1366593' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366593' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366593?labeling=true' target='_blank'>魏郡太守河北采访处置使上党苗公德政碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（747年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366593")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366593_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366593'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366593'>五方殊俗。魏风婉而其人舒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366593_comment'></div>九土异宜。冀田壤而其赋错。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366593_comment'></div>前政有宽猛之异。时令有班艺之差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366593_comment'></div>非夫酌旧典于可行。启新图于必当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366593_comment'></div>多方而不失正。一贯而或从权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366593_comment'></div>曲成便人。大抵厚俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366593_comment'></div>选众而举。非公而谁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366593_comment'></div>公先自吏部侍郎出为安康郡太守。某载月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366593_comment'></div>诏以公为魏郡太守河北道采访处置使。公讳晋卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366593_comment'></div>字元辅。潞州壶关人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366593_comment'></div>其出处本末。奕世冠冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366593_comment'></div>国史家牒详焉。凡邦伯到官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366593_comment'></div>诏使按部。或闭阁思政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366593_comment'></div>或下车作威。或劾吏为明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366593_comment'></div>或移书示禁。公异于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366593_comment'></div>可略而言。公素号贤<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作鲜）</span>明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366593_comment'></div>积有治行。宿讼不决之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366593_comment'></div>馀地割分。疑狱自诬之枉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366593_comment'></div>容光立照。故陋其思政也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366593_comment'></div>安全长吏。不逐老丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366593_comment'></div>成就诸生。先教小吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366593_comment'></div>道德齐礼。有耻且格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366593_comment'></div>故鄙其作威也。谢亭长之问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366593_comment'></div>劳野次之贤。吏悉谓为神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366593_comment'></div>人不隐其毫发。故无事劾吏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366593_comment'></div>列郡共职。清节销其过求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366593_comment'></div>诸曹报薄。直笔破其污诋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366593_comment'></div>故不待移书也。山东古之七雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366593_comment'></div>河北有其四国。地方数千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366593_comment'></div>人盖亿万计。献子三叹之馈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366593_comment'></div>滋无旧德。平原十日之饮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366593_comment'></div>顾有遗风。朱亥袖椎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366593_comment'></div>豪雄扼腕。曹王拂局。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366593_comment'></div>轻薄为心。奢泰拟都护之堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366593_comment'></div>迟缓学邯郸之步。公抑末计<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作技）</span>而敦本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366593_comment'></div>斥浮食以归业。督课八政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366593_comment'></div>择良吏以遣行。讲求六籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366593_comment'></div>置学官于便坐。于是横经左塾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366593_comment'></div>力穑先畴。尽业农桑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366593_comment'></div>大兴庠序。家知礼义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366593_comment'></div>更式段子之庐。户有京坻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366593_comment'></div>增修史起之庙。丛台歌舞成市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366593_comment'></div>邺郡帝王旧都。袨服靓妆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366593_comment'></div>挟筑跕屣。淇上留客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366593_comment'></div>河间数钱。公课其组纴之庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366593_comment'></div>开其婚嫁之节。冶容绝四方之袖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366593_comment'></div>织室致五匹之工。刑于上官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366593_comment'></div>训及处子。郑声卫乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366593_comment'></div>共弃师襄。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_48_1366593", 1366593, "Clauses/97/Comments/0")'>赵带</span>燕裾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366593_comment'></div>思齐漆室。渔阳骑客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366593_comment'></div>奏报本朝。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_50_1366593", 1366593, "Clauses/101/Comments/0")'>鳀海</span>楼船。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366593_comment'></div>连漕绝域。郊迎馆给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366593_comment'></div>不敢淫其刍荛。水路陆衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366593_comment'></div>尽若安于枕席。某载月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366593_comment'></div>诏赐紫袍玉带。金鱼袋衣若干副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366593_comment'></div>方伯十联。赖其澄清之辔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366593_comment'></div>天子七命。赐以安吉之衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366593_comment'></div>缇油屏车。玺书增秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366593_comment'></div>未是过也。胜残之化既成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366593_comment'></div>观俗之风允穆。优游无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366593_comment'></div>学宦思归。况乎父母之邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366593_comment'></div>近在婴儿之国。表请拜扫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366593_comment'></div>有诏许焉。预约守宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366593_comment'></div>幸无侦候。至郡则投刺上谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366593_comment'></div>至邑则舍车而徒。展礼先茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366593_comment'></div>椎心泣血。回趋长老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366593_comment'></div>稽颡绪言。宗人族姻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366593_comment'></div>姑党侄行。觌以重币。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366593_comment'></div>筐篚遍于里闾。享有加牢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366593_comment'></div>牛酒溢于衢陌。朱轩驷马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366593_comment'></div>耀于衡门。紫绶<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_1366593", 1366593, "Clauses/141/Comments/0")'>双龟</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366593_comment'></div>出入编户。苏公佩印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366593_comment'></div>始归乡里尽欢。疏傅散金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366593_comment'></div>不与子孙为计。迨乎将去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366593_comment'></div>仍以馀资。一里置社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366593_comment'></div>备养生送死之具。一乡置校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366593_comment'></div>开说礼敦诗之本。相如衣锦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366593_comment'></div>且飞大汉檄书。买臣怀绶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366593_comment'></div>不德长安厩吏。故使巴蜀太守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366593_comment'></div>负弩前驱。会稽守丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366593_comment'></div>引章下拜。此盖恨不礼于他日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366593_comment'></div>思释憾于故乡。是轻桑梓之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366593_comment'></div>适骋斗筲之志。岂若公自心而至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366593_comment'></div>率礼无违。来悦去思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366593_comment'></div>推才降体。平阳传舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366593_comment'></div>不许望尘。山阴吏卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366593_comment'></div>讵闻治道。富贵还乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366593_comment'></div>荣之至也。扬名显亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1366593_comment'></div>孝之终也。凡百君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1366593_comment'></div>无一至焉。公当<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_89_1366593", 1366593, "Clauses/179/Comments/0")'>九伯</span>之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1366593_comment'></div>兼八使之任。深总之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1366593_comment'></div>不求于无虞。□□□□□□于草窃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1366593_comment'></div>政成德举。风动神行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1366593_comment'></div>顷有勋臣。旁典属郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1366593_comment'></div>曩者风云际会。攀附腾骧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1366593_comment'></div>贪天之功。以为已力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1366593_comment'></div>谓国不忘。尚嘉乃勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1366593_comment'></div>宋父宣骄。条侯倨贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1366593_comment'></div>当关常从。横恣不法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1366593_comment'></div>帷帐狗马。僭侈踰制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1366593_comment'></div>公劾之则重伤国恩。置之则大废邦典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1366593_comment'></div>于是喻以祸福。告之话言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1366593_comment'></div>昔有不爱赵城。将蹈沧海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1366593_comment'></div>既尊汉室。愿遂赤松。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1366593_comment'></div>功成不居。道家所韪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1366593_comment'></div>至于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_105_1366593", 1366593, "Clauses/210/Comments/0")'>析圭分组</span>。跨壤连州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1366593_comment'></div>怀四术而自疑。见九重而失望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1366593_comment'></div>或冤家上变。司败受辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1366593_comment'></div>朝享膏粱。宁知狱吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1366593_comment'></div>暮成菹醢。遍赐诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1366593_comment'></div>难恃白马之盟。徒思黄犬之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1366593_comment'></div>雕墙峻宇。万乘犹惮十愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1366593_comment'></div>紫衣狐裘。一朝而数三罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1366593_comment'></div>虽嫌绛灌等列。不逾梁楚为墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1366593_comment'></div>于是<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_114_1366593", 1366593, "Clauses/228/Comments/0")'>翕肩</span>振惊。折节受教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1366593_comment'></div>杜门谢绝宾客。终身不紊纪纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1366593_comment'></div>以宽服人。实在有德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1366593_comment'></div>厥有挟左道。飞讹言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1366593_comment'></div>南国青珠之符。东海赤刀之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1366593_comment'></div>分风送客。割水饮人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1366593_comment'></div>伪辨而纳之于邪。善诱而济之以恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1366593_comment'></div>户外多保汝之屦。恐为乱阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1366593_comment'></div>门前无长者之车。知其惑众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1366593_comment'></div>公奉诛首恶。悉宥面从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1366593_comment'></div>丕蔽要囚。惟良折狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1366593_comment'></div>议事以制。不徵于书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1366593_comment'></div>副至仁之纳隍。用轻典于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_126_1366593", 1366593, "Clauses/253/Comments/0")'>平国</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1366593_comment'></div>刑期不滥。人乃大安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1366593_comment'></div>奏课计功。天下小察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1366593_comment'></div>责吏以实。则举其不矜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1366593_comment'></div>欲人自新。则贳其宿负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1366593_comment'></div>官以德举。政以礼成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1366593_comment'></div>至于赏善劝能。正源端本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1366593_comment'></div>齐风变鲁。盖以悉礼名儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1366593_comment'></div>晋盗奔秦。岂俟多诛恶少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1366593_comment'></div>纳贡献赋。则惟恐居后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1366593_comment'></div>酬庸命赏。则义不敢先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1366593_comment'></div>布以圣恩。奉宣明主之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1366593_comment'></div>问其理状。对用议曹之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1366593_comment'></div>邦家之光。其斯谓矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1366593_comment'></div>年若干。秀才擢第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1366593_comment'></div>应制举。第若干等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1366593_comment'></div>授某官。历某官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1366593_comment'></div>若夫明眸白皙。玉润珠耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1366593_comment'></div>美秀备于仪形。风流发于言笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1366593_comment'></div>行之方也。留如守司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1366593_comment'></div>智之圆也。速若发括。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1366593_comment'></div>量包群有。思入无间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1366593_comment'></div>坏壁古文。曲台遗礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1366593_comment'></div>淮王九师之易。汉氏三家之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1366593_comment'></div>传癖书淫。鹰扬学府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1366593_comment'></div>比文园入室之武。同丞相登科之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1366593_comment'></div>奏甚平谳。诗穷绮靡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1366593_comment'></div>研燔纸贵。虎视词林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1366593_comment'></div>尝奉和圣制雨中春望诗云。雨后山川光正发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1366593_comment'></div>云端花柳意无穷。又奉和行幸诗云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1366593_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_156_1366593'>接仗风云动。迎军鸟兽舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1366593_comment'></div>时人以为鲍参军谢吏部为更生云。某年月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1366593_comment'></div>诏除公河东太守兼采访使。官吏百姓等或守阙乞留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1366593_comment'></div>或遮道更借。泪增时雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1366593_comment'></div>思结仁风。亲爱之深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1366593_comment'></div>讳名而号为父。歌咏不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1366593_comment'></div>取姓以命其儿。公既去官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1366593_comment'></div>多历年所。人思愈甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1366593_comment'></div>共立生祠。异邑居而瓦合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1366593_comment'></div>无契约而麇至。恐不预于聚财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1366593_comment'></div>惧不任乎输力。棠树勿剪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1366593_comment'></div>何如审像图形。桐乡置祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1366593_comment'></div>岂比耳闻身及。以此观德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1366593_comment'></div>何德之深。仍建丰碑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1366593_comment'></div>立于祠宇。匍匐千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1366593_comment'></div>前后百辈。求缀词之客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1366593_comment'></div>为颂德之文。维也窃比老农。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1366593_comment'></div>不知旧史。众心所至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1366593_comment'></div>难抑与于舆人。予病未能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1366593_comment'></div>不获已于求我。乃为颂曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1366593_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_176_1366593'>禹别九州。汉分八使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1366593_comment'></div>实惟方伯。且曰连帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1366593_comment'></div>建节乘轺。观风察吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1366593_comment'></div>山东河北。全赵大魏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1366593_comment'></div>授方任能。惟名与器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1366593_comment'></div>盖非其才。孰享斯位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1366593_comment'></div>天子命我。导扬皇风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1366593_comment'></div>敬教劝学。通商惠工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1366593_comment'></div>法去太甚。政贵得中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1366593_comment'></div>守丞老病。小吏童蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1366593_comment'></div>督邮不遂。博士成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1366593_comment'></div>遂安贤者。大启儒宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1366593_comment'></div>四国之馀。一都之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1366593_comment'></div>平原旧俗。信陵遗态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1366593_comment'></div>博塞以游。椎埋为害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1366593_comment'></div>丛台淇水。燕裾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_191_1366593", 1366593, "Clauses/383/Comments/0")'>赵带</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1366593_comment'></div>淳化旁属。贞风俶载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1366593_comment'></div>劈纩卷绡。横经秉耒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1366593_comment'></div>清节峻邈。硕量宏深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1366593_comment'></div>投书置水。酹酒捐金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1366593_comment'></div>树德滋蔓。持刑不淫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1366593_comment'></div>讹言免坐。倨贵怀音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1366593_comment'></div>绣衣罢斧。墨绶停琴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1366593_comment'></div>既此时雨。当闻作霖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1366593_comment'></div>申哀松柏。展敬桑梓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1366593_comment'></div>伏谒公门。徒行故里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1366593_comment'></div>椎心马鬣。启颡鲵齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1366593_comment'></div>身纡紫绶。礼及童稚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1366593_comment'></div>帝赐黄金。尽于筐篚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1366593_comment'></div>社养宗人。学招邑子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1366593_comment'></div>能事具举。令问允穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1366593_comment'></div>玺书改印。缇油转毂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1366593_comment'></div>壁挂胡床。舍留官犊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1366593_comment'></div>人吏老幼。涕泗号哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1366593_comment'></div>颂德丰碑。图形华屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1366593_comment'></div>阅实数美。移晷更仆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1366593_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_212_1366593_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=747&endYear=747')">747年</a>　为高仙芝讨小勃律作文。作品：兵部起请露布文。<div id='poem_1366570' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366570' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366570?labeling=true' target='_blank'>兵部起请露布文</a><span class='authorDate'>（747年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366570")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366570_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366570'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366570'>天地之心。无不覆载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366570_comment'></div>鸟鼠之性。自私巢穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366570_comment'></div>国家非徒疆理其地。臣妾其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366570_comment'></div>思欲一车书。混声教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366570_comment'></div>变毒螫之俗。为理义之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366570_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下大道先天。至德冠古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366570_comment'></div>武功则我有七德。文教则舞于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1366570", 1366570, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>两阶</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366570_comment'></div>亿兆广尧封之时。郡县加<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1366570", 1366570, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>禹服</span>之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366570_comment'></div>而犬戎小丑。蜗角偷安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366570_comment'></div>动摇远边。遮汉使之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366570_comment'></div>胁从小国。绝藩臣之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366570_comment'></div>四镇节度使高仙芝等。虔奉圣策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366570_comment'></div>肃将天诛。因识匿之且憎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366570_comment'></div>寻勃律之旧好。暨诸胡国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366570_comment'></div>悉会王师。万里<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1366570", 1366570, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>风驰</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366570_comment'></div>六军电扫。毡裘之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366570_comment'></div>思向风以无阶。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1366570", 1366570, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>毳幕</span>之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366570_comment'></div>惟涂地而可获。遂通重译。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366570_comment'></div>罔不来庭。实赖圣谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366570_comment'></div>曷惟帝力。无攻不克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366570_comment'></div>百蛮皆归于计中。无远不宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366570_comment'></div>万方若在于宇下。臣等不胜喜庆之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366570_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1366570_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=747&endYear=747')">747年</a>　与宋泽交往，有诗。作品：和宋中丞夏日游福贤观天长寺之作。<div id='poem_9252' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9252' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_6_9252'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_9252_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=748&endYear=748')">748年3月</a>　任库部郎中。三月己酉，大同殿柱生玉芝，龙池上有庆云，玄宗赐宴，王维当朝奉官，有诗。作品：大同殿生玉芝龙池上有庆云百官共睹圣恩便赐宴乐敢书即事。<div id='poem_9112' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9112' class='inlineComment2'>（唐玄宗八月五日生，以其生日为千秋节。）</span><div id='poem_9326' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9326' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9326?labeling=true' "王维", "poem_title_9326")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_9326_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_9326'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9326'>太阳升兮照万方，开阊阖兮临玉堂。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9326'>俨冕旒兮垂衣裳，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_9326", 9326, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>金天</span>净兮丽三光。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9326'>彤庭曙兮延八荒，德合天兮礼神遍。<div id='poem_sentence_2_9326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_9326'>灵芝生兮庆云见，唐尧后兮稷卨臣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_9326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_9326'>匝宇宙兮华胥人，尽九服兮皆四邻，乾降瑞兮坤降<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作献）</span>珍。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_9326_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=748&endYear=748')">748年12月2日</a>　十二月二日玄元皇帝降于朝元阁，有诗。作品：奉和圣制登降圣观与宰臣等同望应制。<div id='poem_9329' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9329' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9329?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和圣制登降圣观与宰臣等同望应制</a><span class='authorDate'>（748年12月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_9329")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_9329_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_9329'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9329'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_9329", 9329, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>凤扆</span>朝碧落，龙图耀金镜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9329_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9329'>维岳降二臣，戴天临万姓。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9329_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9329'>山川<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_9329", 9329, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>八校</span>满，井邑三农竟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_9329_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_9329'>比屋皆可封，谁家不相庆。<div id='poem_sentence_3_9329_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_9329'>林疏远村出，野旷寒山静。<div id='poem_sentence_4_9329_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_9329'>帝城云里深，渭水天边映。<div id='poem_sentence_5_9329_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_9329'>佳<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作喜）</span>气含风景，颂声溢歌咏。<div id='poem_sentence_6_9329_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_9329'>端拱能任贤，弥彰圣君圣。<div id='poem_sentence_7_9329_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_9329'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_9329_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=748&endYear=748')">748年</a>　道士申太芝访得古乐器奉进，作贺表。作品：贺古乐器表。<div id='poem_1366546' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366546' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366546?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺古乐器表</a><span class='authorDate'>（748年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366546")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366546_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366546'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366546'>臣维言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366546_comment'></div>伏见今月七日中书门下敕牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366546_comment'></div>道士申太芝奏称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366546_comment'></div>伏奉恩旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366546_comment'></div>令臣往名山修功德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366546_comment'></div>去载六月二十日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366546_comment'></div>于南海葛洪居处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366546_comment'></div>至诚祈请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366546_comment'></div>中夜恍惚见一老人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366546_comment'></div>云是茅山罗浮神人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366546_comment'></div>常于七曜洞来往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366546_comment'></div>昔曾于九疑山桂阳石室中藏天乐一部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366546_comment'></div>岁月久远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366546_comment'></div>变为五野猪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366546_comment'></div>彼郡百姓捉获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366546_comment'></div>汝可往取献皇帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366546_comment'></div>每祈祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366546_comment'></div>但依方安置奏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366546_comment'></div>即五音自和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366546_comment'></div>天仙百神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366546_comment'></div>应声降福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366546_comment'></div>所求必遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366546_comment'></div>寿命延长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366546_comment'></div>臣奉神言即往桂阳寻问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366546_comment'></div>百姓云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366546_comment'></div>天宝二载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366546_comment'></div>村人常见有五野猪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366546_comment'></div>逐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366546_comment'></div>便走入石室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366546_comment'></div>就里寻觅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366546_comment'></div>化为石物五枚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366546_comment'></div>众共惊异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366546_comment'></div>臣取以扣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366546_comment'></div>音律相和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366546_comment'></div>与神人言不异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366546_comment'></div>今将奉进者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366546_comment'></div>臣闻阴阳不测之谓神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366546_comment'></div>变化无方之谓圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366546_comment'></div>唯神与圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366546_comment'></div>感而遂通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366546_comment'></div>伏惟开元天宝圣文神武应道皇帝陛下居皇建之极中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366546_comment'></div>得混成之大道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366546_comment'></div>奉先天之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1366546", 1366546, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>圣祖</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366546_comment'></div>元化协于无为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366546_comment'></div>育率土之群生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366546_comment'></div>至仁侔于阴骘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366546_comment'></div>然犹精意不倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366546_comment'></div>圣祀逾崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366546_comment'></div>遍礼群仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366546_comment'></div>思祐九服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366546_comment'></div>故得厖眉皓发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366546_comment'></div>遥同入昴之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366546_comment'></div>真诀元言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366546_comment'></div>来告驭风之客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366546_comment'></div>栖身七曜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366546_comment'></div>以俟唐尧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366546_comment'></div>藏乐九疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366546_comment'></div>不传虞舜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366546_comment'></div>留兹石室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366546_comment'></div>思献玉墀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366546_comment'></div>凭野豕以呈形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366546_comment'></div>表洞仙之属意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366546_comment'></div>且神物思变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366546_comment'></div>古亦有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366546_comment'></div>龙跃平津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366546_comment'></div>实为宝剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366546_comment'></div>凫飞叶县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366546_comment'></div>空馀素履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366546_comment'></div>器非上品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366546_comment'></div>人才下仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366546_comment'></div>犹能精诚聿修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366546_comment'></div>神变浚若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366546_comment'></div>况殊庭致贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366546_comment'></div>天老效祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366546_comment'></div>愿授至尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366546_comment'></div>以享上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366546_comment'></div>亦既考击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366546_comment'></div>动谐律吕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366546_comment'></div>韶濩惭其九奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366546_comment'></div>云咸失其八音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366546_comment'></div>翠凤入于洞箫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366546_comment'></div>殊非雅韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366546_comment'></div>朱鹭传于鼗鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366546_comment'></div>敢比仙声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366546_comment'></div>天地同和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366546_comment'></div>神祇降福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366546_comment'></div>无穷之寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366546_comment'></div>永抚宝图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1366546_comment'></div>无疆之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1366546_comment'></div>以康庶绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1366546_comment'></div>实由至德斯感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1366546_comment'></div>大道元通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1366546_comment'></div>神人亲告于休徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1366546_comment'></div>灵仙不秘其空乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1366546_comment'></div>稽之古昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1366546_comment'></div>实未见闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1366546_comment'></div>臣等限以留司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1366546_comment'></div>不获随例抃舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1366546_comment'></div>不任踊跃喜庆之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_98_1366546_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=749&endYear=749')">749年</a>　萧嵩卒，作挽歌四首。作品：故太子太师徐公挽歌四首。<div id='poem_9152' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9152' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a
