id='poem_content_9155'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9155'>久践<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_9155", 9155, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>中台</span>座，终登上将坛。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9155'>谁言断车骑，空忆盛衣冠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9155'>风日咸阳惨，笳箫渭水寒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_9155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_9155'>无人当便阙，应罢太师官。<div id='poem_sentence_3_9155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_9155'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_9155_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=749&endYear=749')">749年10月15日</a>　上党郡奏启圣祖大道玄元皇帝玉石真容，作文致贺。作品：贺玄元皇帝见真容表。<div id='poem_1366547' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366547' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366547?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺元元皇帝见真容表</a><span class='authorDate'>（749年10月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366547")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366547_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366547'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366547'>臣维言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366547_comment'></div>伏见中书门下奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366547_comment'></div>上党郡奏启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366547_comment'></div>圣祖大道元元皇帝玉石真容主上圣容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366547_comment'></div>今月十五日三元齐开光明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366547_comment'></div>其日戌后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366547_comment'></div>道士陈希玉等十三人同朝礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366547_comment'></div>见内殿有光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366547_comment'></div>非常照耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366547_comment'></div>及开殿门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366547_comment'></div>其光弥盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366547_comment'></div>满堂如昼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366547_comment'></div>久之方散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366547_comment'></div>其时检校官及押官等皆共瞻睹者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366547_comment'></div>臣闻仙祖行化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366547_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1366547", 1366547, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>真气</span>临关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366547_comment'></div>圣人降生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366547_comment'></div>祥光满室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366547_comment'></div>固知仙圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366547_comment'></div>必有景光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366547_comment'></div>伏惟开元天地大宝圣文神武应道皇帝陛下大道为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366547_comment'></div>上元同体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366547_comment'></div>挟风云之质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366547_comment'></div>敬想犹龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366547_comment'></div>写日月之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366547_comment'></div>钦承大象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366547_comment'></div>仍回旧邸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366547_comment'></div>以奉清都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366547_comment'></div>真容圣容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366547_comment'></div>既明四目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366547_comment'></div>照殿照室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366547_comment'></div>忽类三光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366547_comment'></div>蕊宫自明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366547_comment'></div>初谓上天无夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366547_comment'></div>桂殿如昼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366547_comment'></div>还疑就日而朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366547_comment'></div>琪树韬华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366547_comment'></div>瑶池夺映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366547_comment'></div>实由陛下宏敷本际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366547_comment'></div>大启元宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366547_comment'></div>明君润色于真源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366547_comment'></div>圣祖和光于帝载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366547_comment'></div>表文明之在御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366547_comment'></div>六合以清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366547_comment'></div>知临照之无疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366547_comment'></div>亿载多庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366547_comment'></div>臣等限以留司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366547_comment'></div>不获随例抃舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366547_comment'></div>无任踊跃喜庆之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1366547_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=750&endYear=750')">750年1月</a>　去年七月，于万春乡界频见圣祖空中有言曰：“我以神兵助取石堡城。”作文致贺。作品：贺神兵助取石堡城表。<div id='poem_1366548' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366548' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366548?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺神兵助取石堡城表</a><span class='authorDate'>（750年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366548")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366548_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366548'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366548'>臣维等言。伏奉中书门下牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366548_comment'></div>伏见绛郡太平县百姓王英状称。去载七月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366548_comment'></div>于万春乡界频见圣祖。空中有言曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366548_comment'></div>我以神兵助取石堡城。当时具经郡县陈说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366548_comment'></div>并有文状申奏。讫今载正月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366548_comment'></div>又于旧处再见。云我昔于梓州威洞造一龛<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1366548", 1366548, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>尊像</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366548_comment'></div>在独坐山东北公成山左侧。年代已远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366548_comment'></div>其处倾陷。像在土中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366548_comment'></div>可报吾孙。令人往取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366548_comment'></div>斯乃苍生之福。国祚无疆者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366548_comment'></div>近奉进止。差直省往彼求觅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366548_comment'></div>昨见梓潼郡奏称。去载某月二十六日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366548_comment'></div>郡县官吏并道士父老百姓等一千馀人。与直省李万德依此寻求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366548_comment'></div>其日诸山尽皆晴朗。惟公成山上云雾暗合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366548_comment'></div>遍寻不知所在。遂结坛斋戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366548_comment'></div>祈请经宿。至二十七日辰时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366548_comment'></div>有五色云见于雾合之处。遂即分人子细寻觅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366548_comment'></div>乃见山半腹有少土倾处。其上竹树非常蒙密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366548_comment'></div>并见一石角出土一寸。便穿掘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366548_comment'></div>深三尺已来。乃是一石龛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366548_comment'></div>龛中有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1366548", 1366548, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>尊像</span>一。左右真人六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366548_comment'></div>并师子昆崙各二。遂以水洗沃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366548_comment'></div>仪相俨然。事实吐符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366548_comment'></div>并如真诰。其石龛重大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366548_comment'></div>非人力所能运转。今于龛上造屋宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366548_comment'></div>便差精诚道士三人。专修香火供养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366548_comment'></div>谨画图奉进者。臣闻元德升闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366548_comment'></div>与至降监。必锡灵贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366548_comment'></div>彰厥有成。不秘祥符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366548_comment'></div>昭其克享。伏惟开元天地大宝圣文神武应道皇帝陛下以道理国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366548_comment'></div>以奇用兵。先天而法自然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366548_comment'></div>终日不离辎重。故得仙君居九霄之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366548_comment'></div>屡降中州。圣祖在千古之前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366548_comment'></div>还临后叶。视之不见者今见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366548_comment'></div>听之不闻者今闻。仍敕神兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366548_comment'></div>以助王旅。天丁力士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366548_comment'></div>潜结鹳鹅。星剑云旗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366548_comment'></div>暗充貔虎。遂歼逆命之虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366548_comment'></div>果屠难拔之城。加以言必有徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366548_comment'></div>德无不报。指<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1366548", 1366548, "Clauses/79/Comments/0")'>尊像</span>之所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366548_comment'></div>为宝祚之休徵。周流六虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366548_comment'></div>言于晋而验于蜀。混成一气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366548_comment'></div>出于有而入于无。未达斋心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366548_comment'></div>初迷三里之雾。既符真气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366548_comment'></div>俄成五色之云。山腹洞开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366548_comment'></div>仙容俨若。万物今睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366548_comment'></div>千劫未逢。昔河启绿图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366548_comment'></div>山输元女。尚谓得天之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366548_comment'></div>藏为受命之符。况真诰人闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366548_comment'></div>圣容神造。照临下土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366548_comment'></div>不住大罗之天。保佑群生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366548_comment'></div>爰启小有之洞。实感明主缩地而来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366548_comment'></div>岂比汉时乘空而去。元后<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_52_1366548", 1366548, "Clauses/105/Comments/0")'>钦崇</span>之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366548_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_53_1366548", 1366548, "Clauses/106/Comments/0")'>远至迩安</span>。圣祖昭报之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366548_comment'></div>天长地久。臣等限以留司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366548_comment'></div>不获随例抃舞。不胜踊跃喜庆之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366548_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1366548_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=750&endYear=750')">750年2月</a>　丁母忧，屏居蓝田辋川，诸公来访，有诗酬答。作品：酬诸公见过。<div id='poem_9417' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9417' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_15_9417_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=751&endYear=751')">751年</a>　吴兴郡别驾前京兆尹韩朝宗葬于蓝田白鹿原，为其作墓志铭。作品：唐故京兆君长山公韩府君墓志铭并序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（蜀本《全唐文》载此文，题目作《大唐吴兴郡别驾前荆州大都督府长史山南东道采访使京兆君韩公墓志铭》）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=752&endYear=752')">752年2月</a>　在京。任吏部郎中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=752&endYear=752')">752年3月28日</a>　吏部改为文部，继任文部郎中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=752&endYear=752')">752年4月1日</a>　参加玄宗敕赐百官樱桃盛会，有诗。<div id='poem_9210' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9210' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9210?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕赐百官樱桃<span class='inlineComment2'>（时为文部郎）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（752年4月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_9210")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_9210_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_9210'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9210'>芙蓉阙下会千官，紫禁朱樱出上阑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9210'>才<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作总）</span>是<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_9210", 9210, "Clauses/2/Comments/1")'>寝园</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_9210", 9210, "Clauses/2/Comments/2")'>春荐</span>后，非关御苑鸟衔残。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9210'>归鞍竞带青丝笼，中使频倾赤玉盘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_9210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_9210'>饱食不须愁<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作忧）</span>内热，<span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=752&endYear=752')">752年</a>　秋夜与崔园共同值宿，有诗。作品：同崔员外秋宵寓直。<div id='poem_9124' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9124' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_9124'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9124'>建礼高秋夜，承明候晓过。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9124'><span "Clauses/2/Comments/1")'>寒漏</span>彻，万井<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_9124", 9124, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>曙钟</span>多。<div class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=752&endYear=752')">752年</a>　陆员外往河北，作诗送之。作品：送陆员外。<div id='poem_9359' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9359' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9359?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送陆员外</a><span class='authorDate'>（752年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_9359")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_9359_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_9359'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9359'>郎署有伊人，居然古人风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9359'>天子顾河北，诏书除<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作隶）</span>征东。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9359'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_9359", 9359, id='poem_sentence_3_9359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_9359'>阴风悲枯桑，古塞多飞蓬。<div id='poem_sentence_4_9359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_9359'>万里不见虏，萧条胡地空。<div id='poem_sentence_5_9359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_9359'>无为费中国，更欲邀奇功。<div id='poem_sentence_6_9359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_9359'>迟迟前相送，握手嗟异同。<div id='poem_sentence_7_9359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_9359'>行当封侯归，肯访商山翁。<div id='poem_sentence_8_9359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_9359'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_9359_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=753&endYear=753')">753年</a>　日本遣唐留学生朝衡回国，有诗送行。作品：送秘书朝监还日本国。<span class='inlineComment2'>（朝衡，又作晁衡。）</span><div id='poem_9270' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9270' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9270?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送秘书晁监还日本国</a><span class='authorDate'>（753年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_9270")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_9270_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_9270'>舜觐群后，有苗不格。禹会诸侯，防风后至。动干戚之舞，兴斧钺之诛。乃贡九牧之金，始颁五瑞之玉。我开元天地大宝圣文神武应道皇帝。大道之行，先天布化。乾元广运，涵育无垠。若华为东道之标，戴胜为西门之候。岂甘心于筇杖，非徵贡于包茅。亦由呼耶来朝，舍于葡萄之馆。卑弥遣使，报以蛟龙之锦。牺牲玉帛，以将厚意。服食器用，不宝远物。百神受职，五老告期。况乎戴发含齿，得不稽颡屈膝。海东国，日本为大。服圣人之训，有君子之风。正朔本乎夏时，衣裳同乎汉制。历岁方达，继旧好于行人。滔天无涯，贡方物于天子。同仪加等，位在王侯之先。掌次改观，不居蛮夷之邸。我无尔诈，尔无我虞。彼以好来，废关弛禁。上敷文教，虚至实归。故人民杂居，往来如市。晁司马结发游圣，负笈辞亲。问礼于老聃，学诗于子夏。鲁借车马，孔丘遂适于宗周。郑献缟衣，季札始通于上国。名成太学，官至客卿。必齐之姜，不归娶于高国。在楚犹晋，亦何独于由余。游宦三年，愿以君羹遗母。不居一国，欲其昼锦还乡。庄舄既显而思归，关羽报恩而终去。于是稽首北阙，裹足东辕。箧命赐之衣，怀敬问之诏。金简玉字，传道经于绝域之人。方鼎彝尊，致分器于异姓之国。琅琊台上，回望龙门。碣石馆前，夐然鸟逝。鲸鱼喷浪，则万里倒回。鹢首乘云，则八风却走。扶桑若荠，郁岛如萍。沃白日而簸三山，浮苍天而吞九域。黄雀之风动地，黑蜃之气成云。淼不知其所之，何相思之可寄。嘻。去帝乡之故旧，谒本朝之君臣。咏七子之诗，佩两国之印。恢我王度，谕彼蕃臣。三寸犹在，乐毅辞燕而未老。十年在外，信陵归魏而逾尊。子其行乎，余赠言者。</div><div id='poem_preface_9270_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_9270'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9270'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_9270", 9270, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>积水</span>不可极，安知沧海东。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9270'>九州何处远<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作所）</span>，万里若乘空。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9270'>向国唯看日，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_9270", 9270, "Clauses/5/Comments/1")'>归帆</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（一作途）</span>但信风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_9270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_9270'>鳌身映天黑，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_9270", 9270, "Clauses/7/Comments/1")'>鱼<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作蜃）</span>眼</span>射波红。<div id='poem_sentence_3_9270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_9270'>乡树扶桑外，主人<span id='poem_sentence_0_9365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9365'>君行无几日，当复隔山陂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_9365'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_9365_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=753&endYear=753')">753年9月</a>　同崔兴宗送瑗公返南岳衡山，有诗。作品：同崔宗兴送衡岳瑗公南归并序。<div id='poem_9123' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9123' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9123?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同崔兴宗送衡岳瑗公南归</a><span class='authorDate'>（753年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_9123")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_9123_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_9123'>衡岳瑗上人者，尝学道于五峰，荫松栖云，与狼虎杂处，得无所得矣。天宝癸巳岁，始游于长安。手提瓶笠，至自万里，燕居吐论，缁属高之。初，给事中房公，谪居宜春，与上人风土相接。因为道友，伏腊往来，房公既海内盛名，上人亦以此增价。秋九月，杖锡南返，扣门来别，秦地草木，槭然已黄；苍梧白云，不日而见。滇阳有曹溪学者，为我谢之。</div><div id='poem_preface_9123_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_9123'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9123'>言从石菌阁，新下穆陵关。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9123'>独向池阳去，白云留故山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9123'>绽衣秋日里，洗钵古松间。<div id='poem_sentence_2_9123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_9123'>一施传心法，唯将<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_9123", 9123, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>戒定</span>还。<div id='poem_sentence_3_9123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1366573_comment'></div>传致紫琥之琛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366573_comment'></div>辫发名王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366573_comment'></div>养马于下厩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366573_comment'></div>魋结去帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366573_comment'></div>献珠于小臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366573_comment'></div>而犬戎不识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366573_comment'></div>蜗角自大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366573_comment'></div>偷安九服之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366573_comment'></div>谓天诛罕及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366573_comment'></div>自绝所国之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366573_comment'></div>而王祭不供。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366573_comment'></div>天子按剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366573_comment'></div>谋臣切齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366573_comment'></div>思以赤山为城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366573_comment'></div>青海为堑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366573_comment'></div>尽平其地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366573_comment'></div>悉虏其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366573_comment'></div>而上将有哥舒大夫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366573_comment'></div>名盖四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366573_comment'></div>身长八尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366573_comment'></div>眼如紫石棱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366573_comment'></div>须如猬毛磔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366573_comment'></div>指撝而百蛮不守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366573_comment'></div>叱咤而万人俱废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366573_comment'></div>䯱髵奋髯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366573_comment'></div>哮吼如虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366573_comment'></div>裂眦大怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366573_comment'></div>磨牙欲吞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366573_comment'></div>不待成师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366573_comment'></div>固将<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1366573", 1366573, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>身先士卒</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366573_comment'></div>常思尽敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366573_comment'></div>不以贼遗君父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366573_comment'></div>矢集月窟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366573_comment'></div>剑斩天骄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366573_comment'></div>蹴昆崙使西倒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366573_comment'></div>缚呼韩令北面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366573_comment'></div>岂直赵人祭其东门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366573_comment'></div>匈奴不敢南牧而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366573_comment'></div>开府之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366573_comment'></div>辟书始下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366573_comment'></div>以为踊跃用兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366573_comment'></div>健将之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366573_comment'></div>意气跨马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366573_comment'></div>侠少之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366573_comment'></div>盖欲谋夫起予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366573_comment'></div>哲士俾我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366573_comment'></div>歼黠虏以无类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366573_comment'></div>举外国如拾遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366573_comment'></div>待夷门而不食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366573_comment'></div>置广武于上座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366573_comment'></div>始得我高子焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366573_comment'></div>高子读书五车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366573_comment'></div>运筹百胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366573_comment'></div>慷慨谋议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366573_comment'></div>折天口之是非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366573_comment'></div>指画山川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366573_comment'></div>知地形之要害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366573_comment'></div>尝著七发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366573_comment'></div>曹王慕义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366573_comment'></div>每奏一篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366573_comment'></div>汉文称善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366573_comment'></div>缘情之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366573_comment'></div>独步当时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366573_comment'></div>主人<span class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366573_comment'></div>公卿籍甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366573_comment'></div>遍交欢于五侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366573_comment'></div>孙吴暗合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366573_comment'></div>将建功于万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366573_comment'></div>徵以露版。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1366573_comment'></div>黄云千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1366573_comment'></div>严城落日而闭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1366573_comment'></div>铁骑升山而出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1366573_comment'></div>胡笳咽于塞下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1366573_comment'></div>画角发于军中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1366573_comment'></div>亦可悲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1366573_comment'></div>迟子之献凯云台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1366573_comment'></div>奏事宣室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1366573_comment'></div>紫绶曳地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1366573_comment'></div>金印如斗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_9059_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=755')">755年</a>　房郎中卒于西域，返葬关东，为作祭文。作品：祭兵部房郎中文。<div id='poem_1366607' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366607' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366607?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为人祭兵部房郎中文</a><span class='authorDate'>（755年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366607")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366607_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366607'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366607'>维载月日朔。某官某乙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366607_comment'></div>谨以酒脯之奠。敬祭于故兵部郎中房公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366607_comment'></div>呜呼。君子之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366607_comment'></div>周而不器。苟求行道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366607_comment'></div>未尝私身。沈静好谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366607_comment'></div>话言必雅。往岁谷贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366607_comment'></div>关辅阻饥。眷命自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366607_comment'></div>发廪以赈。中朝乏使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366607_comment'></div>属之鄙夫。不敢自贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366607_comment'></div>请子为介。匹夫嫠妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366607_comment'></div>黄口之孤。钟釜之施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366607_comment'></div>罔不毕当。举无弃粒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366607_comment'></div>野有颂声。国家厌兵革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366607_comment'></div>苦徵戍。大去浮食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366607_comment'></div>以靖国人。单车谕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366607_comment'></div>万里穷碛。西度赤坂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366607_comment'></div>馆于乌孙。形劳者病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366607_comment'></div>神劳则夭。弃成功于末路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366607_comment'></div>未复命而言谢。死不废命忠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366607_comment'></div>尸而加绅宠也。我盥而抚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366607_comment'></div>子瞑受含。求仁得仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366607_comment'></div>其谁不死。玉关之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366607_comment'></div>素车倭迟。愁云昼聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366607_comment'></div>白雪春下。绛旐从风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366607_comment'></div>车徒行哭。至上京而不驻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366607_comment'></div>将返葬于关东。河活活而东注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366607_comment'></div>天惨惨而悲风。道路犹长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366607_comment'></div>子实途穷。人世如旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366607_comment'></div>子实成空。我有旨酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366607_comment'></div>以歆以饯。想像明德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366607_comment'></div>歔欷出涕。尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366607_comment'></div></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=757&endYear=757')">757年10月</a>　广平王收复洛阳后回长安，系于宣阳里杨国忠宅。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=757&endYear=757')">757年12月</a>　付吏议，因以《凝碧诗》闻于肃宗，又弟缙请以己官为之赎罪，特宥之。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='2fff24cc57274c888fe614ea3685526a_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年2月</a>　责授太子中允，上表致谢。作品：谢除太子中允表。<div id='poem_1366550' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366550' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366550?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除太子中允表</a><span class='authorDate'>（758年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1366550'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366550'>臣维稽首言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366550_comment'></div>伏奉某月日制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366550_comment'></div>除臣太子中允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366550_comment'></div>诏出宸衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366550_comment'></div>恩过望表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366550_comment'></div>捧戴惶惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366550_comment'></div>不知所裁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366550_comment'></div>臣闻食君之禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366550_comment'></div>死君之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366550_comment'></div>当逆胡干纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366550_comment'></div>上皇出宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366550_comment'></div>臣进不得从行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366550_comment'></div>退不能自杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366550_comment'></div>情虽可察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366550_comment'></div>罪不容诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366550_comment'></div>伏惟光天文武大圣孝感皇帝陛下孝德动天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366550_comment'></div>圣功冠古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366550_comment'></div>复宗社于坠地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366550_comment'></div>救涂炭于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1366550", 1366550, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>横流</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366550_comment'></div>少康不及君亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366550_comment'></div>光武出于支庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366550_comment'></div>今上皇返正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366550_comment'></div>陛下御乾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366550_comment'></div>历数前王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366550_comment'></div>曾无比德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366550_comment'></div>万灵抃野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366550_comment'></div>六合欢康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366550_comment'></div>仍开祝网之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366550_comment'></div>免臣衅鼓之戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366550_comment'></div>投书削罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366550_comment'></div>端衽立朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366550_comment'></div>秽污残骸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366550_comment'></div>死灭馀气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366550_comment'></div>伏谒明主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366550_comment'></div>岂不自愧于心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366550_comment'></div>仰厕群臣。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366550_comment'></div>且政化之源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366550_comment'></div>刑赏为急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366550_comment'></div>陷身凶虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366550_comment'></div>尚沐官荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366550_comment'></div>陈力兴王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366550_comment'></div>将何宠异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366550_comment'></div>况臣夙有诚愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366550_comment'></div>伏愿陛下中兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366550_comment'></div>逆贼殄灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366550_comment'></div>臣即出家修道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366550_comment'></div>极其精勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366550_comment'></div>庶裨万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366550_comment'></div>顷者身方待罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366550_comment'></div>国未书刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366550_comment'></div>若慕龙象之俦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366550_comment'></div>是避魑魅之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366550_comment'></div>所以钳口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366550_comment'></div>不敢萌心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366550_comment'></div>今圣泽含宏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366550_comment'></div>天波昭洗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366551_comment'></div>擢及无能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366551_comment'></div>恩加非望。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年6月</a>　任给事中。公事之余仍居辋川。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年</a>　秋，请施辋川庄为寺，作文。作品：请施庄为寺表。<div id='poem_1366561' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366561' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366561?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请施庄为寺表</a><span class='authorDate'>（758年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366561")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366561_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366561'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366561'>臣维稽首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366561_comment'></div>臣闻罔极之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366561_comment'></div>岂有能报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366561_comment'></div>终天不返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366561_comment'></div>何堪永思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366561_comment'></div>然要欲强有所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366561_comment'></div>自宽其痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366561_comment'></div>释教有崇树功德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366561_comment'></div>宏济幽冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366561_comment'></div>臣亡母故博陵县君崔氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366561_comment'></div>师事大照禅师三十馀岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366561_comment'></div>褐衣蔬食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366561_comment'></div>持戒安禅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366561_comment'></div>乐住山林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366561_comment'></div>志求寂静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366561_comment'></div>臣遂于蓝田县营山居一所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366561_comment'></div>草堂精舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366561_comment'></div>竹林果园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366561_comment'></div>并是亡亲宴坐之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366561_comment'></div>经行之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366561_comment'></div>臣往丁凶衅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366561_comment'></div>当即发心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366561_comment'></div>愿为伽蓝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366561_comment'></div>永劫追福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366561_comment'></div>比虽未敢陈情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366561_comment'></div>终日常积恳诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366561_comment'></div>又属元圣中兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366561_comment'></div>群生受福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366561_comment'></div>臣至庸朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366561_comment'></div>得备<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1366561", 1366561, id='poem_sentence_31_1366561_comment'></div>愿献如天之寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366561_comment'></div>长为率土之君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366561_comment'></div>惟佛之力可凭。<div id='poem_sentence_36_1366561_comment'></div>固先国而后家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366561_comment'></div>敢以鸟鼠私情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366561_comment'></div>冒触天听。<div id='poem_sentence_41_1366561_comment'></div>精勤禅诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366561_comment'></div>斋戒住持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366561_comment'></div>上报圣恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366555_comment'></div>臣猥以贱伎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366555_comment'></div>得备众工。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366555_comment'></div>无事牸之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366555_comment'></div>徒以职官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366555_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1366556' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366556' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366556?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为曹将军谢写真表</a><span class='authorDate'>（758年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366556")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366556_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366556'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366556'>臣某言。天幸微臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366556_comment'></div>身逢大圣。得为列卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366556_comment'></div>以备戎行。于臣一生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366556_comment'></div>已为万足。况建旗为将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366556_comment'></div>裂组受官。蒙推食之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366556_comment'></div>辱赐衣之宠。匹夫之勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366556_comment'></div>虽不顾身。长策无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366556_comment'></div>未能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1366556", 1366556, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>尽敌</span>。仰惭介冑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366556_comment'></div>俯愧櫜鞬。加以弓不重于六钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366556_comment'></div>箭不穿于七札。讵中雀目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366556_comment'></div>诚惭猿臂。以刘琨而恨小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366556_comment'></div>非关羽之绝伦。何以厕迹虎臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366556_comment'></div>仪形麟阁。伏惟皇帝陛下昭格天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366556_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1366556", 1366556, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>悬超</span>七十二家。微臣托附风云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366556_comment'></div>不如二十八将。而蒙垂圣旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366556_comment'></div>特命图工。画植戟之黄须。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366556_comment'></div>图石棱之紫色。才如过隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366556_comment'></div>顾侯已得其神。不待临淄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366556_comment'></div>邹子自知其丑。岂可藏之秘府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366556_comment'></div>以示后人。将谓飞龙之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366556_comment'></div>无俟貔貅之士。宠过其效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366556_comment'></div>力不称恩。愿死艺于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1366556", 1366556, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>伏韬</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366556_comment'></div>誓杀身于鸣毂。无任感激欣戴之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366556_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1366556_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年</a>　薛使君为婺州刺史，为其作文致谢。作品：为薛使君谢婺州刺史表。<div id='poem_1366553' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366553' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366553?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为嶭使君谢婺州刺史表</a><span class='authorDate'>（758年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366553")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366553_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366553'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366553'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366553_comment'></div>伏奉今月日制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366553_comment'></div>除臣某官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366553_comment'></div>拜命若惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366553_comment'></div>稽首无地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366553_comment'></div>臣闻洪波迅流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366553_comment'></div>必荡其溷秽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366553_comment'></div>庆云所润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366553_comment'></div>不遗于荆棘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366553_comment'></div>伏惟陛下孝悌之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366553_comment'></div>通于神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366553_comment'></div>馨香之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366553_comment'></div>格于天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366553_comment'></div>故指旗而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1366553", 1366553, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>黑祲</span>旋静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366553_comment'></div>挥戈而白日再中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366553_comment'></div>岂臣虫臂鼠肝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366553_comment'></div>所能谈天述圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366553_comment'></div>臣之本末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366553_comment'></div>强欲自陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366553_comment'></div>擢发数罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366553_comment'></div>臣戮馀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366553_comment'></div>剖心自明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366553_comment'></div>天知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366553_comment'></div>臣素书生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366553_comment'></div>少为文吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366553_comment'></div>折冲御侮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366553_comment'></div>几何不亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366553_comment'></div>奉法守文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366553_comment'></div>一日之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366553_comment'></div>当贼逼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1366553", 1366553, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>温洛</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366553_comment'></div>兵接河潼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366553_comment'></div>拜臣陕州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366553_comment'></div>催臣上道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366553_comment'></div>驱马才至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366553_comment'></div>长围已合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366553_comment'></div>未暇施力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366553_comment'></div>旋复陷城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366553_comment'></div>戟枝义头。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366553_comment'></div>刀环筑口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366553_comment'></div>身关木索。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366553_comment'></div>缚就虎狼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366553_comment'></div>臣实惊狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366553_comment'></div>自恨驽怯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366553_comment'></div>脱身虽则无计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366553_comment'></div>自刃有何不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366553_comment'></div>而折节凶顽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366553_comment'></div>偷生厕溷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366553_comment'></div>纵齿盘水之剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366553_comment'></div>未消臣恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366553_comment'></div>空题墓门之石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366553_comment'></div>岂解臣悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366553_comment'></div>今于抱衅之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366553_comment'></div>寄以分忧之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366553_comment'></div>且天兵讨贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366553_comment'></div>曾无汗马之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366553_comment'></div>天命兴王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366553_comment'></div>得返屠羊之肆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366553_comment'></div>免其衅鼓之戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366553_comment'></div>仍开祝网之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366553_comment'></div>臣纵<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_59_1366553", 1366553, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>粉骨糜躯</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366553_comment'></div>不报万分之一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366553_comment'></div>况<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_1366553", 1366553, "Clauses/61/Comments/0")'>褰帷露冕</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366553_comment'></div>是去岁之缧囚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366553_comment'></div>洗垢涤瑕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366553_comment'></div>为圣朝之岳牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366553_comment'></div>臣欲杀身灭愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366553_comment'></div>刎首谢恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366553_comment'></div>生无益于一毛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366553_comment'></div>死何异于腐鼠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366553_comment'></div>谨当闭阁以思政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366553_comment'></div>酌泉以励心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366553_comment'></div>亲毕力于平人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366553_comment'></div>无烦八部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366553_comment'></div>誓不负于明主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366553_comment'></div>非畏四知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366553_comment'></div>用释<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_75_1366553", 1366553, "Clauses/75/Comments/0")'>愆诛</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366553_comment'></div>敢求课最。</div><div id='poem_sentence_76_1366553_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年</a>　韦评事出使北方边塞，有诗送之。作品：送韦评事。<div id='poem_9075' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9075' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9075?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送韦评事</a><span class='authorDate'>（758年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_9075")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_9075_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_9075'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9075'>欲逐将军取<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_9075", 9075, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>右贤</span>，沙场走马向居延。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9075'>遥知汉使萧关外，愁见孤城落日边。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9075'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_9075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_9075'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(9075)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年</a>　韦斌以死明大节，乾元元年肃宗为旌其大节，赠秘书监，为之作神道碑铭并序。作品：大唐故临汝郡太守赠秘书监京兆韦公神道碑铭并序。<div id='poem_1366590' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366590' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366590?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大唐故临汝郡太守赠秘书监京兆韦公神道碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（758年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366590")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366590_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366590'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366590'>坑七族而不顾。赴五鼎而如归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366590_comment'></div>徇千载之名。轻一朝之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366590_comment'></div>烈士之勇也。隐身流涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366590_comment'></div>狱急不见。南冠而絷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366590_comment'></div>逊词以免。北风忽起刎颈送君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366590_comment'></div>智士之勇也。种族其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366590_comment'></div>则废先君之嗣。戮辱及室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366590_comment'></div>则累天子之姻。非苟免以全其生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366590_comment'></div>思得当有以报汉。弃身为饵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366590_comment'></div>俛首入橐。伪就以乱其谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366590_comment'></div>佯愚以折其僭。谢安伺桓温之亟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366590_comment'></div>蔡邕制董卓之邪。然后吞药自裁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366590_comment'></div>呕血而死。仁者之勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366590_comment'></div>夫子为之。公讳斌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366590_comment'></div>字某。京兆杜陵人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366590_comment'></div>昔豕韦氏主盟于商。后扶阳侯重世相汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366590_comment'></div>高祖孝宽。周大司空郧国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366590_comment'></div>曾祖津。陵州刺史寿光县男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366590_comment'></div>祖琬。成州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366590_comment'></div>父安石。左仆射郇国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366590_comment'></div>谥文贞。并勋德茂著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366590_comment'></div>史牒详焉。公即文贞公之仲子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366590_comment'></div>初以宰相子。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1366590", 1366590, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>弁髦</span>署吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366590_comment'></div>抱拜授封。加朝散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366590_comment'></div>封平乐郡公。累拜某官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366590_comment'></div>丁文贞公忧。又丁某国夫人忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366590_comment'></div>无容顾礼。殆不胜丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366590_comment'></div>终身之痛。历稔犹毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366590_comment'></div>幼无童心。长积纯气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366590_comment'></div>抱其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1366590", 1366590, "Clauses/58/Comments/0")'>天素</span>。立于人纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366590_comment'></div>先圣微言。宿儒未辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366590_comment'></div>贯穿精义。总括旁说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366590_comment'></div>文言蔚于舆表。笔态奼于力外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366590_comment'></div>子虚上林。敢云雄似。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366590_comment'></div>黄庭团扇。方议雁行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366590_comment'></div>鹤氅乏姿。羊车夺映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366590_comment'></div>会选公婿。诏婚王室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366590_comment'></div>天家焜耀。独任素风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366590_comment'></div>时论腾踊。宜在右职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366590_comment'></div>乃拜中书舍人。动翔凤之咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366590_comment'></div>启迪古诗。下流水之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366590_comment'></div>敦崇雅诰。转太常少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366590_comment'></div>六宗九奏。悉具其仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366590_comment'></div>天神地祇。可得而礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366590_comment'></div>俄入觐。累贬巴陵太守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366590_comment'></div>稍迁寿春太守。又迁临汝太守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366590_comment'></div>其理务教训。其政尚宽简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366590_comment'></div>谓其叙在六官。又践三事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366590_comment'></div>畴咨帝载。必歌九功之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366590_comment'></div>式和人则。必复三代之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366590_comment'></div>天子避其用亲。奸臣恶其异己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366590_comment'></div>冯衍竟废。扬雄不迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366590_comment'></div>抑古人而有之。何夫子之命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366590_comment'></div>逆贼安禄山。吠尧之犬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366590_comment'></div>驱彼六骡。凭武之狐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366590_comment'></div>犹威百兽。藉天子之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366590_comment'></div>称天子之官。徵天子之兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366590_comment'></div>逆天子之命。始反幽蓟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366590_comment'></div>稍逼温洛。云诛君侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366590_comment'></div>尚惑人心。列郡无备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366590_comment'></div>百司安堵。变折冲为贼矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366590_comment'></div>兼法令而盗之。将逃者已落彀中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366590_comment'></div>谢病者先之死地。密布罗网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366590_comment'></div>遥施陷阱。举足便跌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366590_comment'></div>奋飞即挂。智不能自谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366590_comment'></div>勇无所致力。贼使其骑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366590_comment'></div>劫之以兵。署之以职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366590_comment'></div>以孥为质。遣吏挟行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366590_comment'></div>公溃其腹心。候其间隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366590_comment'></div>义覆元恶。以雪大耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366590_comment'></div>呜呼。上京既骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366590_comment'></div>法驾大迁。天地不仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366590_comment'></div>谷洛方斗。凿齿入骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366590_comment'></div>磨牙食人。君子为投槛之猿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366590_comment'></div>小臣若丧家之狗。伪疾将遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366590_comment'></div>以猜见囚。勺饮不入者一旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366590_comment'></div>秽溺不离者十月。白刃临者四至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366590_comment'></div>赤棒守者五人。刀环筑口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366590_comment'></div>戟枝义颈。缚送贼庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366590_comment'></div>实赖天幸。上帝不降罪疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366590_comment'></div>逆贼恫瘝在身。无暇戮人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366590_comment'></div>自忧为厉。公哀予微节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366590_comment'></div>私予以诚。推食饭我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366590_comment'></div>致馆休我。毕今日欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366590_comment'></div>泣数行下。示予佩玦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366590_comment'></div>斫手长吁。座客更衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366590_comment'></div>附耳而语。指其心曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366590_comment'></div>积愤攻中。流痛成疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1366590_comment'></div>猥不见戮专车之骨。枭枕鼓之头。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1366590_comment'></div>焚骸四衢。然脐三日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1366590_comment'></div>见子而死。知予此心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1366590_comment'></div>言之明日而卒。某年月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1366590_comment'></div>绝于洛阳某之私第。以某月日返葬于某原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1366590_comment'></div>礼也。皇帝中兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1366590_comment'></div>悲怜其意。下诏褒美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1366590_comment'></div>赠秘书监。天下之人谓之赏不失德矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1366590_comment'></div>公敦穆孝友。明允笃诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1366590_comment'></div>高居化源。濡迹物轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1366590_comment'></div>元昆曰陟。伯与仲居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1366590_comment'></div>爱之欲无方。视之若不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1366590_comment'></div>薄其私而厚其室。抑谦已而让其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1366590_comment'></div>故有灵芝耸盖。嘉木连理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1366590_comment'></div>时人以为孝悌之祥。而公昆季谦而不以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1366590_comment'></div>维稚弱之契。晚年弥笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1366590_comment'></div>吾实知之能言者。乃为铭曰<span class='inlineComment2'>（铭亡）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1366590_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_105_1366590_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年</a>　肃宗御题大通（神秀）、大照（普寂）和尚塔额，为舜阇黎作表致谢。作品：为舜阇黎谢御题大通大照和尚塔表。<div id='poem_1366558' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366558' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366558'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366558'>沙门僧某等言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366558_comment'></div>伏蒙圣札题二大师塔额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366558_comment'></div>及度僧抽僧等并毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366558_comment'></div>伏喜天心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366558_comment'></div>俯从人欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366558_comment'></div>恩光至重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366558_comment'></div>抃舞难胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366558_comment'></div>臣闻圣者正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366558_comment'></div>住正法者为圣人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366558_comment'></div>佛者觉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366558_comment'></div>得觉满者入<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1366558", 1366558, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>佛慧</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366558_comment'></div>伏惟光天文武大圣孝感皇帝陛下登满足地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366558_comment'></div>超究竟天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366558_comment'></div>入三解脱门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366558_comment'></div>过九次第定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366558_comment'></div>理事皆如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366558_comment'></div>终非有漏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366558_comment'></div>复皇国而御宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366558_comment'></div>梁鹄惭为古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366558_comment'></div>降出天门。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年</a>　某佛殿上梁，代僧奉表请肃宗赐伞。作品：为僧等请上佛殿梁表。<div id='poem_1366559' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366559' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366559?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为僧等请上佛殿梁表</a><span class='authorDate'>（758年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366559")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366559_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366559'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366559'>僧某言。天地之大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366559_comment'></div>未满法身。绀殿朱宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366559_comment'></div>岂云光宅。陛下尊崇像教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366559_comment'></div>大舍外财。白法利人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366559_comment'></div>黄金布地。不役一人之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366559_comment'></div>不费一家之产。崇崇宝坊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366559_comment'></div>云构将毕。所营某寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366559_comment'></div>以某月日上佛殿梁。伏望天恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366559_comment'></div>内赐一伞。庶使大千世界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366559_comment'></div>悉入盖中。六合人天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366559_comment'></div>共归宇下。然后以无碍慧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366559_comment'></div>大化群物。将使<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1366559", 1366559, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>四生</span>皆度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366559_comment'></div>岂惟比屋可封。则中天之台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366559_comment'></div>才留<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1366559", 1366559, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>幻士</span>。画云之观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366559_comment'></div>徒候神人。以古况今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366559_comment'></div>前王何陋。谨诣右银台门奉表陈请以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366559_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1366559_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年</a>　太子司议郎薛据发此题，有诗。作品：瓜园诗。<div id='poem_9290' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9290' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9290?labeling=true' target='_blank'>瓜园诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（758年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_9290_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_9290'>维瓜园高斋，俯视南山形胜。二三时辈，同赋是诗，兼命词英数公，同用园字为韵。韵任多少，时太子司议郎薛璩发此题，遂同诸公云。</div><div id='poem_preface_9290_comment'></div><div id='poem_allusion_9290_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_9290'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9290'>余适欲锄瓜，倚锄听叩门。<div id='poem_sentence_11_9290_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年</a>　作诗自书复官朝拜时的心情。作品：冬夜书怀。<div id='poem_9289' class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_9289")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_9289_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_9289'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(599, "poem_allusion_9289")'>尚少</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_9289_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_9289'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9289'>冬宵寒且永，夜漏宫中发。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9289'>草白霭繁霜，木衰澄清月。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' "poem_sentence_3_9289")'>尚少</span>，顾影惭朝谒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_9289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_9289'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_9289_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年</a>　奉敕解读帝皇龟镜图，上奏。作品：奉敕详帝皇龟镜图状。<div id='poem_1366562' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366562' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366562?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉敕详帝皇龟镜图状<span class='inlineComment2'>（帝皇龟镜图两卷令简择讫进状）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（758年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366562")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366562_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366562'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366562'>右。某官宣口敕语看可否者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366562_comment'></div>臣愚何足以知。谨与某等议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366562_comment'></div>窃以名为帝皇图者。盖龟可以卜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366562_comment'></div>镜可以照也。以前代帝王行事善恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366562_comment'></div>以卜后代。以前帝王行事善恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366562_comment'></div>以照后代。可以知盛衰兴亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366562_comment'></div>故其行事似尧舜者必盛。似汤武者必兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366562_comment'></div>似秦皇汉武者必衰。似夏桀殷纣者必灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366562_comment'></div>如卜之必知。如照之必见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366562_comment'></div>故谓之龟镜图。伏如所示之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366562_comment'></div>谓之自古帝皇图即可矣。谓之龟镜图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366562_comment'></div>伏恐稍乖名实。又多不出于正经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366562_comment'></div>或取诸子之说。又取曹植飞龙篇挚虞庖牺赞等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366562_comment'></div>是一时文章之语。非正经本传之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366562_comment'></div>至如尧之茅茨不剪。土阶三尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366562_comment'></div>就之如日。望之如云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366562_comment'></div>舜之逐窜四凶。举<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1366562", 1366562, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>十六族</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366562_comment'></div>臣歌九德。君抚五弦等善事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366562_comment'></div>夏桀之瑶台琼室。殷纣之肉林酒池等恶事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366562_comment'></div>盖画如此之类。乃成龟镜之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366562_comment'></div>至于伏羲生时。伏羲之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366562_comment'></div>女娲肠化。搏土为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366562_comment'></div>如此之流。岂为龟镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366562_comment'></div>若记帝皇之事。总载无妨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366562_comment'></div>若为龟镜之图。恐须简择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366562_comment'></div>又论元气已后。其图似重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366562_comment'></div>太初与太始无殊。有形与有质不异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366562_comment'></div>易云乾元亨利贞。即未有物者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366562_comment'></div>乾之始也。乾者元之体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366562_comment'></div>元者乾之用也。上犹道家旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366562_comment'></div>道生一。一生二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366562_comment'></div>二生三。三生万物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366562_comment'></div>又近佛经八识。是清净无所有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366562_comment'></div>第八识即含藏一切种子。第六识即分别成五阴十八界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366562_comment'></div>此图从元气已下。名目稍多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366562_comment'></div>臣识用愚浅。不知忌讳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366562_comment'></div>敢率鄙见。无任战越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366562_comment'></div>伏惟圣心裁择。谨状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366562_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1366562_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=759&endYear=759')">759年</a>　任给事中。钱起归蓝田，有诗赠之。作品：春夜竹亭赠钱少府归蓝田。<div id='poem_9342' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9342' class='poemTitle id='poem_content_9342'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9342'>夜静群动息，时闻隔林犬。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9342'>却忆山中时，人家涧西远。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9342'>羡君<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_9342", 9342, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>明发</span>去，采蕨轻轩冕。<div id='poem_sentence_2_9342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_9354'>慷慨念王室，从容献<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_9354", 9354, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>官箴</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_9354_comment'></div></div><div
