ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=759&endYear=759')">759年</a>　惠干和尚集解《仁王般若经》十卷进上肃宗，王维为之写表。作品：为干和尚进注仁王经表。<div id='poem_1366557' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366557' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366557?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为干和尚进注仁王经表</a><span class='authorDate'>（759年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366557")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366557_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366557'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366557'>沙门惠干言。法离言说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366557_comment'></div>了言说即解脱者。终日可言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366557_comment'></div>法无名相。知名相即真如者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366557_comment'></div>何尝坏相。实际以无际可示。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366557_comment'></div>无生以不生相传。非夫自得性空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366557_comment'></div>密印心地。见闻自在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366557_comment'></div>宗说皆通者。何以證玉毫之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366557_comment'></div>辩<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1366557", 1366557, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>金口</span>之义。伏惟乾元大圣光天文武孝感皇帝陛下高登十地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366557_comment'></div>降抚九天。宏济群生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366557_comment'></div>濡莲花之足。示行世法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366557_comment'></div>屈金粟之身。心净超禅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366557_comment'></div>顶法悬解。广释门之六度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366557_comment'></div>包儒行之五常。老僧空空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366557_comment'></div>复何<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1366557", 1366557, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>语语</span>。以无见之见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366557_comment'></div>不言之言。浅智胜疑冰之虫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366557_comment'></div>微戒愈溺泥之象。以自觉离念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366557_comment'></div>注先圣微言。如人<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑一作麻）</span>何足尽思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366557_comment'></div>食木偶然成字。岂堪上尘慧眼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366557_comment'></div>仰称圣心。有命自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366557_comment'></div>藏拙无地。伏以集解仁王般若经十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366557_comment'></div>谨随笔奉进。无任惭惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366557_comment'></div>然本注经。先发大愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366557_comment'></div>释第一义。开不二门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366557_comment'></div>与四十九僧。离一百八句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366557_comment'></div>六时禅诵。三载恳祈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366557_comment'></div>俾廓祅氛。得瞻慧日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366557_comment'></div>三千世界。悉奉神王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366557_comment'></div>五千善神。常卫乐土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366557_comment'></div>今果荡定。无量安宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366557_comment'></div>缁服苍生。不胜庆跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366557_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1366557_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=759&endYear=759')">759年</a>　作裴遵庆画像赞。作品：裴右丞写真赞。<div id='poem_1366587' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366587' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366587?labeling=true' target='_blank'>裴右丞写真赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（759年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366587")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1366587_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366587'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366587'>澹尔清德，居然素风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1366587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1366587'>气和容众，心静如空。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1366587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1366587'>智以穷理，才包至公。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1366587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1366587'>大盗振骇，群臣困蒙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1366587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1366587'>忘身徇节，历险能通。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1366587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1366587'>仁者之勇，义无失忠。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1366587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1366587'>凝情取象，惟雅则同。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1366587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1366587'>粉绘不及，清明在躬。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1366587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1366587'>麟阁之上，其谁比崇。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1366587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1366587'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1366587_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=759&endYear=759')">759年</a>　任给事中。作品：与魏居士书。<div id='poem_1366568' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366568' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366568?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与魏居士书</a><span class='authorDate'>（759年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366568")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366568_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366568'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366568'>足下太师之后。世有明德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366568_comment'></div>宜其四代五公。克复旧业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366568_comment'></div>而伯仲诸昆。顷或早世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366568_comment'></div>唯有寿光。复遭播越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366568_comment'></div>幼生弱侄。藐然诸孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366568_comment'></div>布衣徒步。降在皂隶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366568_comment'></div>足下不忍其亲。杖策入关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366568_comment'></div>降志屈体。托于所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366568_comment'></div>身不衣帛。而于六亲孝慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366568_comment'></div>终日一饭。而以百口为累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366568_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1366568", 1366568, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>攻苦食淡</span>。流汗霢霂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366568_comment'></div>为之驱驰。仆见足下裂裳毁冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366568_comment'></div>二十馀年。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1366568", 1366568, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>山栖谷饮</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366568_comment'></div>高居深视。造次不违于仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366568_comment'></div>举止必由于道。高世之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366568_comment'></div>欲盖而彰。又属圣主搜扬仄陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366568_comment'></div>束帛加璧。被于岩穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366568_comment'></div>相国急贤。以副旁求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366568_comment'></div>朝闻夕拜。片善一能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366568_comment'></div>垂章拖组。况足下崇德茂绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366568_comment'></div>清节冠世。风高于黔娄善卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366568_comment'></div>行独于石门荷蓧。朝廷所以超拜右史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366568_comment'></div>思其入践赤墀。执牍珥笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366568_comment'></div>羽仪当朝。为天子文明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366568_comment'></div>且又禄及其室养。昆弟免于负薪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366568_comment'></div>樵苏晚爨。柴门闭于积雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366568_comment'></div>藜床穿而未起。若有称职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366568_comment'></div>上有致君之盛。下有厚俗之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366568_comment'></div>亦何顾影跼步。行歌采薇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366568_comment'></div>是怀宝迷邦。爱身贱物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366568_comment'></div>岂谓足下利钟釜之禄。荣数尺之绶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366568_comment'></div>虽方丈盈前。而蔬食菜羹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366568_comment'></div>虽高门甲第。而毕竟空寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366568_comment'></div>人莫不相爱。而观身如聚沫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366568_comment'></div>人莫不自厚。而视财若浮云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366568_comment'></div>于足下实何有哉。圣人知身不足有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366568_comment'></div>故曰欲洁其身而乱大伦。知名无所著也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366568_comment'></div>故曰欲使如来名声普闻。故离身而返屈其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366568_comment'></div>知名空而返不避其名也。古之高者曰许由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366568_comment'></div>挂瓢于树。风吹瓢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366568_comment'></div>恶而去之。闻尧让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366568_comment'></div>临水而洗其耳。耳非驻声之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366568_comment'></div>声无染耳之迹。恶外者垢内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366568_comment'></div>病物者自我。此尚不能至于旷士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366568_comment'></div>岂入道者之门欤。降及嵇康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366568_comment'></div>亦云顿缨狂顾。逾思长林而忆丰草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366568_comment'></div>顿缨狂顾。岂与俛受维絷有异乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366568_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1366568", 1366568, "Clauses/94/Comments/0")'>长林丰草</span>。岂与官署门阑有异乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366568_comment'></div>异见起而正性隐。色事碍而慧用微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366568_comment'></div>岂等同虚空。无所不遍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366568_comment'></div>光明遍照。知见独存之旨邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366568_comment'></div>此又足下之所知也。近有陶潜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366568_comment'></div>不肯把板屈腰见督邮。解印绶弃官去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366568_comment'></div>后贫乞食诗云。叩门拙言词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366568_comment'></div>是屡乞而多惭也。尝一见督邮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366568_comment'></div>安食公田数顷。一惭之不忍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366568_comment'></div>而终身惭乎。此亦人我攻中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366568_comment'></div>忘大守小。不□其后之累也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366568_comment'></div>孔宣父云。我则异于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366568_comment'></div>无可无不可。可者适意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366568_comment'></div>不可者不适意也。君子以布仁施义活国济人为适意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366568_comment'></div>纵其道不行。亦无意为不适意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366568_comment'></div>苟身心相离。理事俱如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366568_comment'></div>则何往而不适。此近于不易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366568_comment'></div>愿足下思可不可之旨。以种类俱生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366568_comment'></div>无行作以为大依。无守嘿以为绝尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366568_comment'></div>以不动为出世也。仆年且六十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366568_comment'></div>足力不强。上不能原本理体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366568_comment'></div>裨补国朝。下不能殖货聚谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366568_comment'></div>博施穷窘。偷禄苟活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366568_comment'></div>诚罪人也。然才不出众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366568_comment'></div>德在人下。存●去就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366568_comment'></div>如<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_72_1366568", 1366568, "Clauses/144/Comments/0")'>九牛一毛</span>耳。实非欲引尸祝以自助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366568_comment'></div>求分谤于高贤也。略陈起予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366568_comment'></div>惟审图之。维白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366568_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_75_1366568_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=759&endYear=759')">759年</a>　王欤因孝而家生紫芝木瓜，献于朝廷，为之作赞并序。作品：为相国王公紫芝木瓜赞并序。<div id='poem_1366585' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366585' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366585?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为相国王公紫芝木瓜赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（759年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366585")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1366585_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1366585'>孝悌之至。通于神明。天为之降和。地为之嘉植。发书占之。推理可得。何者。人心本于元气。元气被于造物。心善者气应。气应者物美。故呈祥于鱼鸟。或发挥于草木。示神明之阴骘。与天地之嘉会。今中书侍郎相公先生左丞府君。沈潜上德。遐尚绝轨。江海漭沆。婴孩杏坛。高门长轨。隐几含素。盖凤凰之高逝。薄龙虎之逶迤。积有淳德。诞敷馀庆。而我相公生而英姿。河目海口。量与太素。而无端倪。应会神速。动若发括。事遣理尽。澹然虚空。亦犹太清。云无处所。重元之旨。达而有馀奥。太白之明。漫而不及理。文可以经邦训俗。武可以保大定功。故天子咨之。以布元化。昔者高堂既。扇枕无所。呕血长号。礼不能制其哭泣之度。终身巨痛。时无以加其霜露之惕。攻苦食淡。寝苫枕块。泪少于血。骨馀于形。风唳起而裂其心。鸟悲鸣而感其哭。俄而紫芝生栋。叶若(一作华成)仙人之盖。色夺齐侯之衣。又有木瓜在林。味若楚王之萍。大如安期之枣。枯木无生物之理。而布濩滋蔓。时果有常分之形。而硕大殊尤。邻里骇之。郡县闻之。公泣而不敢言。州司遽表以献。或曰。因心而致。人之祥也。或曰。率土所生。国之瑞也。有识君子曰。至孝所感。物为人之祥。大贤佐时。人为国之瑞。二物者。虽感曩时之纯至。亦符今日之崇高也。公尤不敢当。归美于今上。以为震位先兆。孝德动天。至乾元二年。乃画图以进。诏报曰。芝草者。延寿之徵也。木瓜者。投报之应也。盖至诚所感。有开必先。朕与卿道契云龙。义同水石。位崇台衮。寄重股肱。故得嘉瑞荐臻。灵物昭格。君臣同德。区宇克宁。览其进图。可为嘉应。请宣付史馆者。既依史策。亦藏书府。赞曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1366585_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366585'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366585'>紫芝三秀，则生于梁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1366585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1366585'>木瓜一实，其大盈筐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1366585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1366585'>嘉应荐至，其故何祥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1366585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1366585'>哀哀孝思，涟涟泣血。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1366585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1366585'>终身致毁，每恸将绝。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1366585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1366585'>云为裴回，风为惨切。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1366585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1366585'>依仁据德，移孝为忠。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1366585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1366585'>经目尽理，任心便公。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1366585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1366585'>其道橐籥，虚而不穷。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1366585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1366585'>公位先兆，圣人斯睹。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1366585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1366585'>赐以诏书，藏之秘府。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1366585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1366585'>邦家之光，哀荣终古。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1366585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1366585'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1366585_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>　拜尚书右丞。严武任河南尹，返回长安与王维会晤，有诗。作品：河南严尹弟见宿敝庐访别人赋十韵。<div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_9261'>花醥<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作醴）</span>和松屑<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，茶香透竹丛。<div id='poem_sentence_4_9261_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_note_9261_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>　请将前两职中书舍人给事中之一司职田粟施与贫人粥。作品：请回前任司职田粟施贫人粥状。<div id='poem_1366563' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366563' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366563?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请回前任司职田粟施贫人粥状</a><span class='authorDate'>（760年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366563")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366563_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366563'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366563'>右。臣比见道路之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366563_comment'></div>冻馁之人。朝尚呻吟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366563_comment'></div>暮填沟壑。陛下圣慈怜悯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366563_comment'></div>煮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1366563", 1366563, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>公粥</span>施之。顷年已来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366563_comment'></div>多有全济。至仁之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366563_comment'></div>感动上天。故得年谷颇登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366563_comment'></div>逆贼皆灭。报施之应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366563_comment'></div>福祐昭然。臣前任中书舍人给事中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366563_comment'></div>两任职田。并合交纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366563_comment'></div>近奉恩敕。不许并请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366563_comment'></div>望将一司职田。回与施粥之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366563_comment'></div>于国家不减数粒。在穷窘或得再生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366563_comment'></div>庶以上福圣躬。永宏宝祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366563_comment'></div>仍望令刘晏分付所由讫。具数奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366563_comment'></div>如圣恩允许。请降墨敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366563_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1366563_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>　肃宗大赦天下，为颁行赦书事代门下省官员作奏天。作品：门下起赦书表。<div id='poem_1366549' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366549' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366549?labeling=true' target='_blank'>门下起赦书表</a><span class='authorDate'>（760年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366549")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366549_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366549'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366549'>伏奉制书如右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366549_comment'></div>好生之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366549_comment'></div>洽于人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366549_comment'></div>奉天之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366549_comment'></div>以行春令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366549_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1366549", 1366549, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>体元</span>作则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366549_comment'></div>惟圣裁成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366549_comment'></div>伏惟乾元大圣光天文武孝感皇帝陛下道凝庶绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366549_comment'></div>功深广运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366549_comment'></div>极孝敬于至诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366549_comment'></div>致雍和于允穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366549_comment'></div>狭其祝网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366549_comment'></div>陋彼画衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366549_comment'></div>宁失不经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366549_comment'></div>况乎轻系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366549_comment'></div>大赦戮馀之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366549_comment'></div>益宽流宥之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366549_comment'></div>人谓无冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366549_comment'></div>何如舍而不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366549_comment'></div>杀而有礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366549_comment'></div>岂若至于无刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366549_comment'></div>加以亲减庶羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366549_comment'></div>无祭肺之膳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366549_comment'></div>下除冗食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366549_comment'></div>赡糊口之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366549_comment'></div>买椟设楬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366549_comment'></div>藏彼无归之骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366549_comment'></div>岁取亩收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366549_comment'></div>本乎盍彻之税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366549_comment'></div>巨猾止于一恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366549_comment'></div>贫人免于十夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366549_comment'></div>思折券者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366549_comment'></div>宽其暴征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366549_comment'></div>尝书勋者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366549_comment'></div>贳其宿负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366549_comment'></div>道德齐礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366549_comment'></div>成其有耻之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366549_comment'></div>悔咎思愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366549_comment'></div>风俗忠厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366549_comment'></div>礼让兴行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366549_comment'></div>六府孔修。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>　作文送冯少府赴任郓州须昌。作品：送郓州须昌冯少府赴任序。<div id='poem_1366576' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366576' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366576_comment'></div>辅之以才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366576_comment'></div>大官大邑可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366576_comment'></div>不惟是欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366576_comment'></div>予昔仕鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366576_comment'></div>盖尝之郓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366576_comment'></div>书社万室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366576_comment'></div>带以鱼山济水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366576_comment'></div>旗亭千隧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366576_comment'></div>杂以郑商周客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366576_comment'></div>有邹人之风以厚俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366576_comment'></div>不耽乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366576_comment'></div>不弄法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366576_comment'></div>不慢官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366576_comment'></div>无侮老成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366576_comment'></div>无虐孤与幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366576_comment'></div>上官奏课。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366576_comment'></div>輶轩以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366576_comment'></div>则绣衣方领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366576_comment'></div>垂珰珥笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366576_comment'></div>子所得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366576_comment'></div>谁敢有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366576_comment'></div>予病且惫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366576_comment'></div>岁晚弥独。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366576_comment'></div>穷巷衡门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366576_comment'></div>落日秋草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366576_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1366576", 1366576, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>赵服</span>过我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366576_comment'></div>且东其辕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366576_comment'></div>促饭中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366576_comment'></div>子不可以蔬食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366576_comment'></div>送车出郭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366576_comment'></div>吾不可以徒行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366576_comment'></div>屦以及门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366576_comment'></div>拜于宇下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366576_comment'></div>犹且抱杖延颈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366576_comment'></div>送之以目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366576_comment'></div>城回树转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366576_comment'></div>悲其马嘶云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1366576_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>　感年老力衰，自料不久于人事，思念胞弟缙，责躬荐弟，愿归所任官，放田里，使缙得还京师。作品：责躬荐弟表。<div id='poem_1366560' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366560' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366560?labeling=true' target='_blank'>责躬荐弟表</a><span class='authorDate'>（760年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366560'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366560'>臣维稽首言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366560_comment'></div>臣年老力衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366560_comment'></div>心昏眼暗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366560_comment'></div>自料涯分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366560_comment'></div>其能几何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366560_comment'></div>久窃天官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366560_comment'></div>每惭尸素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366560_comment'></div>顷又没于逆贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366560_comment'></div>不能杀身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366560_comment'></div>负国偷生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366560_comment'></div>以至今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366560_comment'></div>陛下矜其愚弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366560_comment'></div>托病被囚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366560_comment'></div>不赐疵瑕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366560_comment'></div>屡迁<span id='poem_sentence_16_1366560_comment'></div>在于微臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366560_comment'></div>百生万足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366560_comment'></div>昔在贼地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366560_comment'></div>始愿屡违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366560_comment'></div>私心自咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366560_comment'></div>为政本原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366560_comment'></div>非敢议论他人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366560_comment'></div>窃以兄弟自比。<div id='poem_sentence_40_1366560_comment'></div>尽心为国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366560_comment'></div>竭力守城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366560_comment'></div>臣即陷在贼中。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>　作诗酬张少府。<div id='poem_9226' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9226' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9226?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_9322'>晚知清净理，日与人群疏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9322'>将候远山僧，先期埽弊庐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9322'>果从云峰里，顾我蓬蒿居。<div id='poem_sentence_2_9322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_9322'>藉草饭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_9322", 9322, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>松屑</span>，焚香看道书。<div id='poem_sentence_3_9322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_9322'>然灯昼欲尽，鸣磬夜方初。<div id='poem_sentence_4_9322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_9322'>一悟寂为乐，此日<span onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_9322", 9322, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>空虚</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_9322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_9322'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_9322_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=761&endYear=761')">761年5月4日</a>　肃宗答王维《责躬荐弟表》诏书下，上状致谢。作品：谢弟缙新授左散骑常侍状。<div id='poem_1366564' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366564' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366564'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366564'>右。臣之兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366564_comment'></div>皆迫桑榆。每至一别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366564_comment'></div>恐难再见。匪躬之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366564_comment'></div>诚不顾家。临老之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366564_comment'></div>实悲远道。陛下均平布政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366564_comment'></div>中外遰迁。尚录前劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366564_comment'></div>仍收旧齿。使备顾问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366564_comment'></div>载珥貂蝉。趋侍玉墀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366564_comment'></div>从容琐闼。不材之木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366564_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1366564", 1366564, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>跗萼联芳</span>。断行之雁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366564_comment'></div>飞鸣接翼。自天之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366564_comment'></div>特出宸衷。涂地之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366564_comment'></div>难酬圣造。不胜戴荷踊跃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366564_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1366564_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=761&endYear=761')">761年</a>　维辞官后，慕容承送素馔，维写诗以酬。作品：慕容承携素馔见过。<div id='poem_9231' 洛阳

id='poem_title_1366592' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366592?labeling=true' target='_blank'>京兆尹张公德政碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（734年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1366592_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366592'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366592'>云从龙。风从虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366592_comment'></div>气应也。圣人作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366592_comment'></div>贤人辅。德同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366592_comment'></div>君臣同德。天地通气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366592_comment'></div>以康九有。以遂万类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366592_comment'></div>惟皇御极二十载。光格四表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366592_comment'></div>至于海隅日出。越小大邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366592_comment'></div>蛮貊师长。罔不钦于成宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366592_comment'></div>以承天休。然天子犹日省三揖<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作接）</span>列辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366592_comment'></div>日听万方舆颂。惧人有未化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366592_comment'></div>贤有未登。故扬仄陋兼乎十等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366592_comment'></div>选宗室及乎九族。任事以观材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366592_comment'></div>积时以观行。乃得我贤京兆焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366592_comment'></div>夫京兆号为难理。清净病于不给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366592_comment'></div>刀笔拘于守文。或以软弱废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366592_comment'></div>或以贼杀劾。把宿负浅为丈夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366592_comment'></div>用钩距盖非长者。我则异于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366592_comment'></div>大道难名。大理无法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366592_comment'></div>闭关于任数。巧算不能知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366592_comment'></div>坚壁于画一。善政不能下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366592_comment'></div>摧宿豪如薙草。无愠色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366592_comment'></div>视大权如历块。无傲容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366592_comment'></div>百司之务<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作吏）</span>。总以奇而得正<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作总一德以咸服）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366592_comment'></div>五方之人。杂异教而同理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366592_comment'></div>受命之始。先声已振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366592_comment'></div>黠吏恶少。闻风改行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366592_comment'></div>及乎鸣驺诣府。登堂坐定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366592_comment'></div>县尹掾史。以次上谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366592_comment'></div>守正之人其气高。含章之人其词大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366592_comment'></div>见容色而闻号令。小人戚而君子泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366592_comment'></div>日者栎阳男子。闾里为豪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366592_comment'></div>借客报仇。聚人为盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366592_comment'></div>或白日手刃。或黄尘袖椎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366592_comment'></div>政宽则以身先诸偷。操急则以事中长吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366592_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1366592", 1366592, "Clauses/68/Comments/0")'>贰过</span>不已。万计自脱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366592_comment'></div>公命吏缚之。立死铃下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366592_comment'></div>于是人入闇室。若遇大宾焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366592_comment'></div>前年不登。人悴太甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366592_comment'></div>野无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1366592", 1366592, "Clauses/76/Comments/0")'>遗秉</span>。路有委骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366592_comment'></div>天子不忍征于不粒。赋于无衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366592_comment'></div>六军从卫。以临东诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366592_comment'></div>息关中也。帝曰咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366592_comment'></div>天其降威。人罔畏罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366592_comment'></div>台恐寇盗乃邑。矧曰荡析离居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366592_comment'></div>惟尔克济。抚兹方夏<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作西土）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366592_comment'></div>公拜稽首。思塞休命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366592_comment'></div>布慈惠之政。不以利淫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366592_comment'></div>振雷霆之威。其或宥过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366592_comment'></div>饔人减双鸡之膳。圉人省五马之秣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366592_comment'></div>陶不献服。圬不塓馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366592_comment'></div>自身已往。振廪同食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366592_comment'></div>虽人烟不动。道殣相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366592_comment'></div>不思滥以苟生。咸守教以就死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366592_comment'></div>是不可能也。先是王公或专南山之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366592_comment'></div>司农涸昆明之池。收赤岸泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366592_comment'></div>将为田以便官。至是悉奏罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366592_comment'></div>舟鲛衡麓之守废。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_56_1366592", 1366592, "Clauses/113/Comments/0")'>蒲荷</span>薪蒸之产入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366592_comment'></div>自郊徂邑。室有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_57_1366592", 1366592, "Clauses/115/Comments/0")'>鱼飧</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366592_comment'></div>斩阴伐阳。市多山木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366592_comment'></div>人得以赡。唯泾有防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366592_comment'></div>比岁多决。近县疲于力役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366592_comment'></div>他山匮于度林。公命刮朽壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366592_comment'></div>填巨石。办大木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366592_comment'></div>去<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_63_1366592", 1366592, "Clauses/126/Comments/0")'>编菅</span>。其始告劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366592_comment'></div>乃终有庆。匠石日减功万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366592_comment'></div>藏史日省钱亿。农始竟耒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366592_comment'></div>女始安织。于是台背黄发之老曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366592_comment'></div>我有田畴。钟秉其亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366592_comment'></div>我有子弟。颜闵其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366592_comment'></div>乡党以睦。茕失其独。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366592_comment'></div>道路有礼。汰无与争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366592_comment'></div>酒先养老。贿不问吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366592_comment'></div>既无犬吠。亦无奸人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366592_comment'></div>临年馀资。幸蒙惠化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366592_comment'></div>其曷以臻兹。君子曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366592_comment'></div>此天子至公。内举不避亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366592_comment'></div>锡汝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_76_1366592", 1366592, "Clauses/152/Comments/0")'>明尹</span>。张公之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366592_comment'></div>夫公于国为外戚。于帝为外弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366592_comment'></div>重组累印。珥香貂者七叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366592_comment'></div>奉车驸马。乘朱轮者十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366592_comment'></div>胜衣则绮襦纨裤。通籍则玉墀青琐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366592_comment'></div>动则两骖如舞。坐则五鼎成列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366592_comment'></div>文轩楚制。素女赵舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366592_comment'></div>而公俨兮其若客。澹兮其无味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366592_comment'></div>心在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_84_1366592", 1366592, "Clauses/168/Comments/0")'>四教</span>。语称七德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366592_comment'></div>目视六籍。口诵九歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366592_comment'></div>怀君子令德之忠。保诗人锡类之孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366592_comment'></div>悌有过于共被。慈有踰于含食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1366592_comment'></div>恶衣以居。公服不敢降也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1366592_comment'></div>屈体下士。王网不敢替也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1366592_comment'></div>协二姓之好以正人伦。旁无嬖御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1366592_comment'></div>分一人之忧以审官政。下多英杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1366592_comment'></div>若夫皇帝敬问之诏。御札自书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1366592_comment'></div>天王命赐之衣。上宫所制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1366592_comment'></div>劳勤则中使接武。计议则走马来朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1366592_comment'></div>岂惟众臣重其经术。为吏杂以儒雅而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1366592_comment'></div>且公之<span class='inlineComment2'>（一有德字）</span>升闻于天。非一朝一夕之渐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1366592_comment'></div>亦以称职于累官。著声于所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1366592_comment'></div>其丞秘书也。阙文<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_98_1366592", 1366592, "Clauses/197/Comments/0")'>遗简</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1366592_comment'></div>多在大家。深为子孙之藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1366592_comment'></div>密有缄滕之固。公不惮权贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1366592_comment'></div>或抵或诱。尽归天阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1366592_comment'></div>官书备焉。其牧郢也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1366592_comment'></div>人有不若德。戮之不为暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1366592_comment'></div>人有不保居。抚之不为謟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1366592_comment'></div>存者考其事壮其食以畜之。行者缉其宫艺其树以待之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1366592_comment'></div>此邦之人既优。他邦之人又重<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作至）</span>焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1366592_comment'></div>未盈一岁。遂增万户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1366592_comment'></div>其守汾也。仍岁大旱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1366592_comment'></div>郡祠介推。虽屡舞仙仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1366592_comment'></div>而灵应未若。公命束缊取火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1366592_comment'></div>伐树寘薪。酾酒而祝曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1366592_comment'></div>有功于人。祀为明神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1366592_comment'></div>无德而禄。祸亦覆餗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1366592_comment'></div>自绛以来。人实祀子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1366592_comment'></div>纯牺大璧不敢爱。必以荐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1366592_comment'></div>童男季女不敢黩。必以敬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1366592_comment'></div>神既靡答。人将安仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1366592_comment'></div>若亭午而雨。则树其鹭羽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1366592_comment'></div>执此骍毛。不然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1366592_comment'></div>火燎将至。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_120_1366592", 1366592, "Clauses/241/Comments/0")'>焮天铄地</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1366592_comment'></div>灵衣且为煨烬。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_121_1366592", 1366592, "Clauses/243/Comments/0")'>丰屋</span>将为茂草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1366592_comment'></div>尔其图之。言未毕而云兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1366592_comment'></div>拜未起而雨降。周于阖境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1366592_comment'></div>不入他郡。虽封疆咫尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1366592_comment'></div>而彼竭我盈。嘻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1366592_comment'></div>若记能事。载盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1366592_comment'></div>渭川之竹不足简。终南之木不足轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1366592_comment'></div>夫训人至于礼义曰德。安人免于阽危曰功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1366592_comment'></div>功德者。上赏于上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1366592_comment'></div>下颂于下。长老孜孜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1366592_comment'></div>愿刊于石。以予学于旧史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1366592_comment'></div>来即我谋。且维与人编户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1366592_comment'></div>与人为伍。与人出入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1366592_comment'></div>与人言语。知风俗之淳毙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1366592_comment'></div>识政化之源本。属词愧文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1366592_comment'></div>书事盖实。词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1366592_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_137_1366592'>五代相韩。七叶侍汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1366592_comment'></div>及我圣朝。亦生<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_138_1366592", 1366592, "Clauses/277/Comments/0")'>邦翰</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1366592_comment'></div>大道无形。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_139_1366592", 1366592, "Clauses/279/Comments/0")'>贞蛊</span>以干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1366592_comment'></div>含章不耀。在割能断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1366592_comment'></div>情伪万端。吾道一贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1366592_comment'></div>帝选贤尹。无以易张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1366592_comment'></div>金印紫绶。京兆之良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1366592_comment'></div>佩我鸣玉。冠我两梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1366592_comment'></div>天子休命。拜手以将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1366592_comment'></div>宽而爱人。立灭暴强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1366592_comment'></div>明明天子。哀此南亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1366592_comment'></div>将息西人。遂觐东后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1366592_comment'></div>我教我训。我镇我守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1366592_comment'></div>茫茫三秦。则罔糊口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1366592_comment'></div>守死以义。徇生不苟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1366592_comment'></div>王曰外弟。视人不佻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1366592_comment'></div>何以宠之。手书以诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1366592_comment'></div>何以问之。赐衣而朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1366592_comment'></div>俾人华胥。致君帝尧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1366592_comment'></div>刻石作颂。永世弥昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1366592_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_157_1366592_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='6f36b90baf0e42479ee63fe4720b5fd9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6f36b90baf0e42479ee63fe4720b5fd9");'><span id='6f36b90baf0e42479ee63fe4720b5fd9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>，36岁</div><div id='6f36b90baf0e42479ee63fe4720b5fd9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年3月9日</a>　张九龄进封始兴县开国子，献诗。作品：献始兴公。<div id='poem_9402' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9402' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9402?labeling=true' target='_blank'>献始兴公<span class='inlineComment2'>（时拜右拾遗）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（735年3月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_9402")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_9402_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_9402'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3393, "poem_allusion_9402")'>公器</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_9402_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_9402'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9402'>宁栖野树林，宁饮涧水<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作中）</span>流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9402_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9402'>不用坐粱肉，崎岖见王侯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9402_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9402'>鄙哉匹夫节，布褐将白头。<div id='poem_sentence_2_9402_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_9402'>任智诚则短，守任固其优。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=725&endYear=725')">725年</a>　与济州刺史裴耀卿交往。作品：和使君五郎西楼望远思归。<div id='poem_9324' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9324' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9324?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和使君五郎西楼望远思归</a><span class='authorDate'>（725年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_9324")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_9324_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_9324'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9324'>高楼望所思，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_9324", 9324, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>目极</span>情未毕。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9324_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9324'>枕上见千里，窗中窥万室。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9324_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9324'>悠悠长路人，暧暧远郊日。<div id='poem_sentence_2_9324_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_9324'>惆怅极浦外，迢递孤烟出。<div id='poem_sentence_3_9324_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_9324'>能赋属上才，思归同<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_9324", 9324, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>下秩</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_9324_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_9324'>故乡不可见，云水<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作外）</span>空如一。<div id='poem_sentence_5_9324_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_9324'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_9324_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=726&endYear=726')">726年</a>　裴耀卿离任济州刺史，济州百姓为裴立功德碑，维作碑文。作品：裴仆射济州遗爱碑并序。<div id='poem_1366591' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366591' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366591?labeling=true' target='_blank'>裴仆射齐州遗爱碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（726年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366591")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366591_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366591'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366591'>夫为政以德。必世而后仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366591_comment'></div>齐人以刑。苟免而无耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366591_comment'></div>则刑禁者难久。百年安可胜残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366591_comment'></div>德化者效迟。三载如何考绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366591_comment'></div>刑以助德。猛以济宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366591_comment'></div>期月政成。成而不朽者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366591_comment'></div>惟公能之。公名耀卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366591_comment'></div>字涣之。河东闻喜人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366591_comment'></div>益为帝虞。实相帝舜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366591_comment'></div>非子其冑。而邑诸裴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366591_comment'></div>在汉者为水衡。在魏者守代郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366591_comment'></div>十三代祖徽。魏益豫雍兖徐五州刺史兰陵武公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366591_comment'></div>源于大贤。派以俊德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366591_comment'></div>世济其美。不陨其名矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366591_comment'></div>曾祖正。隋散骑常侍长平郡赞理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366591_comment'></div>祖慎。皇朝洛南南郑二县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366591_comment'></div>著族斯茂。衣冠未敢争雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366591_comment'></div>继世皆贤。英彦无出其右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366591_comment'></div>故有常侍县君。递辉迭映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366591_comment'></div>父守真。太常博士判驾部夏官员外今上楚王府咨议参军邠宁二州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366591_comment'></div>赠晋兖沂三州刺史。文儒之宗伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366591_comment'></div>礼乐之本源。藉业虽曰承家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366591_comment'></div>复始由乎种德。再典大郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366591_comment'></div>二为仙郎。举十大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366591_comment'></div>是则是敩。且年不及寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366591_comment'></div>而位未称德。朝多其能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366591_comment'></div>殁而独赠。公则晋州之第三子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366591_comment'></div>语而能文。有识便知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366591_comment'></div>为儿则量过黄发。未仕而心在苍生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366591_comment'></div>伯达试经。子炎应诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366591_comment'></div>古之人也。我不后之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366591_comment'></div>八岁神童举。试毛诗尚书论语及第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366591_comment'></div>解褐补秘书省校书郎。历睿宗安国相王府典签。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366591_comment'></div>东观载笔。班固名香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366591_comment'></div>西园赋咏。刘桢气逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366591_comment'></div>转国子主簿检校詹事府丞。学识宜在儒林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366591_comment'></div>风度雅膺储寀。河南府士曹参军考功员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366591_comment'></div>公府屈廊庙之才。曹无留事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366591_comment'></div>仙郎明黜陟之法。野无遗贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366591_comment'></div>右司兵部二郎中长安县令。其在含香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366591_comment'></div>一台推妙。以之制锦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366591_comment'></div>四海是仪。公之断狱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366591_comment'></div>必原情以定罪。不阿意以侮法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366591_comment'></div>是以小失天旨。出为此州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366591_comment'></div>公推善于国。不称无罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366591_comment'></div>思利于人。志其屈已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366591_comment'></div>戮豪右以惩恶。一至无刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366591_comment'></div>旌孝弟以劝善。洪惟见德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366591_comment'></div>然后务材训农。通商惠工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366591_comment'></div>敬教劝学。授方任能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366591_comment'></div>行之一年。郡乃大理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366591_comment'></div>襁负而至。何忧乎荡析之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366591_comment'></div>路不拾遗。何畏乎穿窬之盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366591_comment'></div>既富之矣。汲黯奚取于开仓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366591_comment'></div>使无讼乎。仲由何施其折狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366591_comment'></div>居无何。诏封东岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366591_comment'></div>关东列郡。颇当驰道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366591_comment'></div>至于牺牲玉帛。资粮屝屡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366591_comment'></div>其或不供。为有司所劾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366591_comment'></div>因而厚敛。非天子之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366591_comment'></div>丰省之度。多不得中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366591_comment'></div>故二千石有不能受事于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_1366591", 1366591, "Clauses/122/Comments/0")'>宰旅</span>者矣。季孙请鲁视邾滕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366591_comment'></div>涛涂恐师出陈郑。抑为是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366591_comment'></div>公尽事君之心。且曰从人之欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366591_comment'></div>万斯箱之粟。兹乃如京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366591_comment'></div>百执事之人。于我乎馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366591_comment'></div>四封之境。二为帝庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366591_comment'></div>一郡之赋。再粒天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366591_comment'></div>士卒<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_68_1366591", 1366591, "Clauses/136/Comments/0")'>林会</span>。马牛谷量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366591_comment'></div>皆投足获安。端拱取给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366591_comment'></div>无虞燥湿。不畏寇盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366591_comment'></div>草莽之中。用能便其体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366591_comment'></div>羁绁之外。无所劳其力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366591_comment'></div>天朝中贵。持权用事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366591_comment'></div>厚为之礼。则生我<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_74_1366591", 1366591, "Clauses/149/Comments/0")'>羽毛</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366591_comment'></div>小不如意。则成是贝锦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366591_comment'></div>公享有常牢。觌无私币。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366591_comment'></div>冒货贿者。我以为仇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366591_comment'></div>淫刍荛者。吾所能御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366591_comment'></div>至于急宣中旨。暴征庶物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366591_comment'></div>或命嘉蔬。先春当荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366591_comment'></div>锡贡珍果。非土所生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366591_comment'></div>举是一隅。其徒千计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366591_comment'></div>皆曾不旋踵。若取诸怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366591_comment'></div>又不知其备预之所以然也。谓饩牢竭矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366591_comment'></div>而家有馀粮。谓疲劳甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366591_comment'></div>而人有馀力。岂非积年之储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366591_comment'></div>用之有度。终身之逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1366591_comment'></div>使之有时。不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1366591_comment'></div>班贡艺事。轻重以列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1366591_comment'></div>我视子男之国。而倍公侯之征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1366591_comment'></div>今日之事。我为上也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1366591_comment'></div>大驾还都。分遣中丞蒋钦绪御史刘日政宋珣等巡按。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1366591_comment'></div>皆嘉公之能。奏课第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1366591_comment'></div>公未受赏。朝而归藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1366591_comment'></div>天灾流行。河水决溢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1366591_comment'></div>蝗虫避境。虽马棱之化能然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1366591_comment'></div>洪水滔天。固帝尧之时且尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1366591_comment'></div>高岸萃以云断。平郊豁其地裂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1366591_comment'></div>喷薄雷吼。冲融天回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1366591_comment'></div>百姓巢居。主客有其家室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1366591_comment'></div>五稼波殄。沼毛荒于畎亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1366591_comment'></div>公急人之虞。分帝之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1366591_comment'></div>御衣假寐。对案辍食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1366591_comment'></div>不候驾而星迈。不入门而雨行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1366591_comment'></div>议堤防也。至则平板干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1366591_comment'></div>具糇粮。揆形略趾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1366591_comment'></div>量功命日。而赤岸成谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1366591_comment'></div>白涛亘山。虽有吕梁之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1366591_comment'></div>尽下淇园之竹。无能为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1366591_comment'></div>乃有坏防之馀。冲波且尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1366591_comment'></div>仅在而危同累卵。将坠而间不容发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1366591_comment'></div>公暴露其上。为人请命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1366591_comment'></div>风伯屏气以迁迹。阳侯整波而退舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1366591_comment'></div>又王尊至诚。未足加也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1366591_comment'></div>然后下密楗。搴长茭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1366591_comment'></div>土篑云积。金锤电散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1366591_comment'></div>公亲巡而抚之。慰而勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1366591_comment'></div>千夫毕饭。始就饮食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1366591_comment'></div>一人未息。不归蘧庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1366591_comment'></div>惰者发愤以跞勤。懦者自强以齐壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1366591_comment'></div>成之不日。金堤峨峨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1366591_comment'></div>下截重泉。上可方轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1366591_comment'></div>北河回其竹箭。东郡郁为桑田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1366591_comment'></div>先是朝廷除公宣州刺史。公惜九仞之垂成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1366591_comment'></div>恐众心之或怠。怀丝纶之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1366591_comment'></div>密金玉之音。率负薪而益勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1366591_comment'></div>亲执扑而弥励。既成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1366591_comment'></div>乃发书示之。皆舍畚攀辕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1366591_comment'></div>废歌成泣。泪洏济袂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1366591_comment'></div>泽阴鲁郊。哀哀号呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1366591_comment'></div>不崇朝而达四境。噫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1366591_comment'></div>公之视人也如子。人之去公也如父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1366591_comment'></div>宜其升闻于天。司我五教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1366591_comment'></div>公之富人也以简。简则不扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1366591_comment'></div>而人得肄其业。非富欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1366591_comment'></div>公之爱吏也以严。严则畏威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1366591_comment'></div>而吏不陷于罪。非爱欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1366591_comment'></div>是其大旨也。至若沛郡谓为神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1366591_comment'></div>淮阳谢其清净。尊经于学校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1366591_comment'></div>鲁风载儒。加信于儿童。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1366591_comment'></div>齐人不诈。明閒视听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1366591_comment'></div>其察奸也无全。晓习文法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1366591_comment'></div>于决事乎何有。六义之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1366591_comment'></div>文在于斯。五车之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1366591_comment'></div>学半于我。其为身计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1366591_comment'></div>保乎忠贞。将为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_146_1366591", 1366591, "Clauses/293/Comments/0")'>孙谋</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1366591_comment'></div>贻以清白。熊轼之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1366591_comment'></div>子弟夷于平人。龙门则高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1366591_comment'></div>宾客不遗下士。非礼不动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1366591_comment'></div>出言有章。语曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1366591_comment'></div>恺悌君子。人之父母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1366591_comment'></div>其是之谓乎。维也不才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1366591_comment'></div>尝备官属。公之行事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1366591_comment'></div>岂不然乎。维实知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1366591_comment'></div>维能言之。况夫妇男女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1366591_comment'></div>思我遗爱者。唫咏成风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1366591_comment'></div>耆艾人吏。愿颂清德者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1366591_comment'></div>道路如市。则王褒所讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1366591_comment'></div>奚斯之颂。美政盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1366591_comment'></div>缀词之士。固未尝阙如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1366591_comment'></div>维敢拒之哉。颂曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1366591_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_162_1366591'>童子何知兮公迈成人。大不必佳兮公德日新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1366591_comment'></div>天生德于公兮遗此下民。天子命我兮守兹东郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1366591_comment'></div>人调公以谪去兮不能致训。公曾不私已兮政声益振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1366591_comment'></div>惟岁十月兮帝封岱宗。千乘万骑兮行幸山东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1366591_comment'></div>小郡之赋兮再粒万邦。丰不盈俭不陋兮公之举也得中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1366591_comment'></div>河为不道兮离常流以痡毒。不用一牲兮不沈一王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1366591_comment'></div>身当中流兮冯夷感而避贤。敕阳侯兮使却走夫洪涟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1366591_comment'></div>板筑既具兮薪又属。庶人欣以就役兮高岸崛起于深谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1366591_comment'></div>人降邱宅土兮桑田郁以载绿。行无五马兮食不载味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1366591_comment'></div>惠恤鳏寡兮威詟黠吏。公之德兮曾无与二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1366591_comment'></div>人思遗爱兮泪淫淫。岁久不衰兮至今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1366591_comment'></div>性与天道吾不得闻兮。志其小者近者兮已是过人之德音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1366591_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_174_1366591_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
泰安（乾封）
-----detail

class='inlineComment2'>（一作载）</span>馀，五岳遍曾居。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9281_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9281'>遥识齐侯鼎，新过<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(29, "poem_sentence_1_9281")'>王母</span>庐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9281_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9281'>不能师<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5294, "poem_sentence_2_9281")'>孔墨</span>，何事问长沮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_9281_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_9281'>玉管时来凤，铜盘即钓鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_9281_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_9281'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_9281", 9281, 清河
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ee7d0874a5654ecb9a9d46dd1344cd37_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ee7d0874a5654ecb9a9d46dd1344cd37");'><span id='ee7d0874a5654ecb9a9d46dd1344cd37_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=723&endYear=723')">723年</a>，24岁</div><div id='ee7d0874a5654ecb9a9d46dd1344cd37' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=723&endYear=723')">723年</a>　贬济州，游齐、鲁、冀一带，与道士、隐者、贤者交往，有诗。作品：渡河到清河作。<div id='poem_9390' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9390' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9390?labeling=true' target='_blank'>渡河到清河作</a><span class='authorDate'>（723年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_9390")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_9390_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_9390'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9390'>汎舟大河里，积水穷天涯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9390'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_9390", 9390, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>天波</span>忽开拆，郡邑千万家。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9390'>行复见城市，宛然有桑麻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_9390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_9390'>回瞻旧乡国，淼漫连云霞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_9390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_9390'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_9390_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

"poem_sentence_3_9173")'>饮月氏头</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_9173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_9173'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_9173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_9173'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(9173)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><div id='poem_9090' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9090' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9090?labeling=true' target='_blank'>渭城曲<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup> 送元二使安西</a><span class='authorDate'>（738年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_9090")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_9090_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_9090_0'>① 《渭城》一曰《阳关》，王维之所作也。本送人使安西诗，后遂被于歌。刘禹锡《与歌者诗》云“旧人唯有何戡在，更与慇勤唱渭城”，白居易《对酒诗》云“相逢且莫推辞醉，听唱阳关第四声。即劝君更尽一杯酒，西出阳关无故人”也。渭城、阳关之名，盖因辞云。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_9090'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9090'>渭城朝雨浥轻尘，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_9090", 9090, "Clauses/1/Comments/2")'>客舍</span>青青<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作依依）</span>杨柳春<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作柳色新）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9090_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9090'>劝君更尽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_9090", 9090, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>一杯</span>酒，西出<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_9090", 9090, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>阳关</span>无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_9090", 9090, -----title
南京（江宁）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0e70d0d915ec4320b82d7d4150f5a920_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0e70d0d915ec4320b82d7d4150f5a920");'><span id='0e70d0d915ec4320b82d7d4150f5a920_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=741&endYear=741')">741年2月</a>　到瓦官寺拜谒璿上人，有诗。<div id='poem_9386' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9386' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9386?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谒璿上人</a><span class='authorDate'>（741年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_9386")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_9386_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_9386'>上人外人内天，不定不乱，舍法而渊泊；无心而云动，色空无碍，不物物也；默语无际，不言言也。故吾徒得神交焉。玄关大启，德海群泳，时雨既降，春物具美。序于诗者，人百其言。</div><div id='poem_preface_9386_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_9386'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1951, "poem_allusion_9386")'>阮家屐</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(7834, id='poem_sentence_0_9386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9386'>事往安可悔，馀生幸能养。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9386'>誓从断臂<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作荤）</span>血，不复婴世网。<div id='poem_sentence_2_9386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_9386'>浮名寄<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_9386", 9386, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>缨佩</span>，空性无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_9386", 9386, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>羁鞅</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_9386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_9386'>夙承<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作从）</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_9386", 9386, "Clauses/8/Comments/1")'>大导师</span>，焚香此<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_9386", 9386, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>瞻仰</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_9386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_9386'>颓然居一室，覆载纷万象。<div id='poem_sentence_5_9386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_9386'>高柳早莺啼，长廊春雨响。<div id='poem_sentence_6_9386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_9386'>床下<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1951, "poem_sentence_7_9386")'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_9386", 9386, "Clauses/14/Comments/1")'>阮家屐</span></span>，窗前筇竹杖。<div id='poem_sentence_7_9386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_9386'>方将见<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_9386", 9386, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>身云</span>，陋彼<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(7834, "poem_sentence_8_9386")'>示天壤</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_9386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_9386'>一心在法要，愿以无生奖。<div id='poem_sentence_9_9386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_9386'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_9386_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

九江

-----title
蓝田
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0ab17b5059f944f4ba2e7fe1313eb30c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0ab17b5059f944f4ba2e7fe1313eb30c");'><span id='0ab17b5059f944f4ba2e7fe1313eb30c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=744&endYear=744')">744年</a>，45岁</div><div id='0ab17b5059f944f4ba2e7fe1313eb30c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=744&endYear=744')">744年</a>　任库部员外郎。作品：辋川集二十首。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='3102b254cb994de8a541efabc97fa4cf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3102b254cb994de8a541efabc97fa4cf");'><span id='3102b254cb994de8a541efabc97fa4cf_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年</a>，59岁</div><div id='3102b254cb994de8a541efabc97fa4cf' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>闲居蓝田辋川，李遵遣人慰问，作书以示感激。作品：与工部李侍郎书。<div id='poem_1366566' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366566' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366566?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与工部李侍郎书</a><span class='authorDate'>（758年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_1366566")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366566_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366566'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366566'>一昨出后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366566_comment'></div>伏承令从官将军车骑至陋巷见命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366566_comment'></div>恨不得随使者诣舍下谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366566_comment'></div>才非张载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366566_comment'></div>枉傅元以车相迎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366566_comment'></div>德谢侯生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366566_comment'></div>辱信陵虚左见待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366566_comment'></div>古人有此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366566_comment'></div>今也未闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366566_comment'></div>所以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1366566", 1366566, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>竦踊</span>惕息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366566_comment'></div>通夕不寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366566_comment'></div>维自结发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366566_comment'></div>即枉眷顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366566_comment'></div>侍郎素风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366566_comment'></div>维知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366566_comment'></div>宿昔贵公子常下交布衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366566_comment'></div>尽礼髦士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366566_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1366566", 1366566, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>绝甘分少</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366566_comment'></div>致醴以饭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366566_comment'></div>汲汲于当世之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366566_comment'></div>常如不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366566_comment'></div>故夙著闻望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366566_comment'></div>为孟尝平原之俦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366566_comment'></div>及乎晚岁时危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366566_comment'></div>益见臣节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366566_comment'></div>草莽之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366566_comment'></div>乘舆播越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366566_comment'></div>列郡或<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1366566", 1366566, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>弃车走林</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366566_comment'></div>畏贼顾望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366566_comment'></div>贡献不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366566_comment'></div>莫有斗心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366566_comment'></div>侍郎慨然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366566_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1366566", 1366566, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>枕戈泣血</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366566_comment'></div>奋不顾命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366566_comment'></div>捍卫圣主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366566_comment'></div>杨奉之以兵奉迎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366566_comment'></div>萧何之运粮致馈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366566_comment'></div>曹洪之以良马济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366566_comment'></div>赵衰之以壶飧从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366566_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1366566", 1366566, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>收合</span>亡骑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366566_comment'></div>缮治兵甲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366566_comment'></div>喻以大义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366566_comment'></div>慰而勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366566_comment'></div>然后以剑率卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366566_comment'></div>执戈前驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366566_comment'></div>浃旬之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366566_comment'></div>六军响振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366566_comment'></div>以成兴复之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366566_comment'></div>岂非侍郎忠节盖世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366566_comment'></div>义贯白日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366566_comment'></div>垂名竹帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366566_comment'></div>为一代宗臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366566_comment'></div>诚可爱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366566_comment'></div>或曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366566_comment'></div>宗子与国同休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366566_comment'></div>不得不尔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366566_comment'></div>夫仁弱自爱者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366566_comment'></div>且奔窜伏匿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366566_comment'></div>偷延晷刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366566_comment'></div>穷蹙既至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366566_comment'></div>即匹夫匹妇自经于沟渎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366566_comment'></div>安能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_1366566", 1366566, "Clauses/61/Comments/0")'>决命争首</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366566_comment'></div>慷慨大节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366566_comment'></div>死生以之乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366566_comment'></div>而能不邀宠于上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366566_comment'></div>不干功于下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366566_comment'></div>不怠邦政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366566_comment'></div>不受私谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366566_comment'></div>时与风流儒雅之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366566_comment'></div>置酒高会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366566_comment'></div>唫咏先王遗风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366566_comment'></div>翛然有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_71_1366566", 1366566, "Clauses/71/Comments/0")'>东山之志</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366566_comment'></div>善矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366566_comment'></div>维虽老贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366566_comment'></div>沈迹无状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366566_comment'></div>岂不知有忠义之士乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366566_comment'></div>亦常延颈企踵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366566_comment'></div>向风慕义无穷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366566_comment'></div>然不敢自列于下执事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366566_comment'></div>以为贱贵有伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366566_comment'></div>等威有序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366566_comment'></div>以閒人持不急之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366566_comment'></div>朝夕<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_82_1366566", 1366566, "Clauses/82/Comments/0")'>倚门窥户</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366566_comment'></div>抑亦侍郎之所恶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366566_comment'></div>而猥不见遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366566_comment'></div>思曹公命吴质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366566_comment'></div>将何以塞知已之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366566_comment'></div>报厚顾之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1366566_comment'></div>内省空虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1366566_comment'></div>流汗而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1366566_comment'></div>辄先驰状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1366566_comment'></div>候凉时即躬诣门下奉谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1366566_comment'></div>王维顿首。</div><div id='poem_sentence_92_1366566_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>闲居蓝田辋川，以诗自遣。作品：辋川别业。<div id='poem_9219' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9219' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9219?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辋川别业</a><span class='authorDate'>（758年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_9219")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_9219_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_9219'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2204, "poem_allusion_9219")'>倒屣</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(10162, "poem_allusion_9219")'>伛偻丈人</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_9219_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_9219'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9219'>不到东山向一年，归来才及种<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_9219", 9219, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>春田</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9219_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9219'>雨中草色绿堪染，水上桃花红欲<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作亦）</span>然。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9219_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9219'>优娄比丘<span "poem_sentence_2_9219")'>伛偻丈人</span>乡里贤。<div id='poem_sentence_2_9219_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_9219'>披衣<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2204, id='poem_sentence_4_9219_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
准格尔旗（榆林）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fbc03bbb931c43d49d96ec95b046faed_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fbc03bbb931c43d49d96ec95b046faed");'><span id='fbc03bbb931c43d49d96ec95b046faed_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=745&endYear=745')">745年</a>，46岁</div><div id='fbc03bbb931c43d49d96ec95b046faed' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=745&endYear=745')">745年</a>　出使榆林，有诗。作品：榆林郡歌。<div id='poem_9401' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9401' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9401?labeling=true' target='_blank'>榆林郡歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（745年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_9401")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_9401_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_9401'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9401'>山头松柏林，山下泉声伤客心。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9401'>千里万里春草色，黄河东流流不息。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9401'>黄龙戍上游侠儿，愁逢汉使不相识。<div id='poem_sentence_2_9401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_9401'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_9401_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
神木（新秦）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='84afd6a8646f489a938406afc529ff7e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("84afd6a8646f489a938406afc529ff7e");'><span id='84afd6a8646f489a938406afc529ff7e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=745&endYear=745')">745年</a>，46岁</div><div id='84afd6a8646f489a938406afc529ff7e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=745&endYear=745')">745年</a>　出使新秦，有诗。作品：新秦郡松树歌。<div id='poem_9399' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_9399' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/9399?labeling=true' target='_blank'>新秦郡松树歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（745年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18616, "盛唐", "王维", "poem_title_9399")'>王维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_9399_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_9399'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_9399'>青青山上松，数里不见今更逢。<div id='poem_sentence_0_9399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_9399'>不见君，心相忆，此心向君君应识。<div id='poem_sentence_1_9399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_9399'>为君颜色高且闲，亭亭迥出浮云间。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_9399_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
